# Council of Ministers / Majlis Al-Wuzara <orig>مجلس الوزراء</orig>
## Decree-Law No. 61 of 2025
### Extending the Period Stipulated in Law No. 3 of 2016 Authorizing the Government to Withdraw an Amount from the General Reserve Fund

- Having reviewed the Constitution,
- And Amiri Order <orig>الأمر الأميري</orig> issued on 2 Dhu al-Qi'dah 1445 AH, corresponding to May 10, 2024 AD,
- And Law No. 24 of 1963 regarding the establishment of the Supreme Defense Council <orig>مجلس الدفاع الأعلى</orig>, amended by Decree-Law No. 53 of 1987,
- And Decree-Law No. 31 of 1978 regarding the rules for preparing general budgets, monitoring their implementation, and the final account, and its amending laws,
- And Decree-Law No. 27 of 1981 regarding increasing the amounts allocated for strengthening the country's defense, amended by Decree-Law No. 33 of 1987,
- And Decree-Law No. 35 of 1988 regarding increasing the amounts allocated for strengthening the country's defense,
- And Decree-Law No. 46 of 1992 regarding increasing the amounts allocated for strengthening the country's defense, and its amending laws,
- And Law No. 3 of 2016 authorizing the Government to withdraw an amount from the General Reserve Fund <orig>المال الاحتياطي العام</orig>,
- And Decree No. 84 of 2024 concerning Ministerial Succession and Delegation <orig>الحلول والإنابات الوزارية</orig>, and its amending decrees,
- And based on the presentation by the Minister of Defense <orig>عرض وزير الدفاع</orig>,
- And after the approval of the Council of Ministers / Majlis Al-Wuzara <orig>مجلس الوزراء</orig>,
- We have issued the following Decree-Law:

### Article One
The period stipulated in Articles One and Two of the aforementioned Law No. 3 of 2016 shall be extended for an additional two fiscal years.
<page_end>1</page_end>

Kuwait Today / Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig> Issue 1733, Seventy-First Year
2
Sunday, 8 Shawwal 1446 AH – 6/4/2025 AD
</header>

### Article Two
The Prime Minister <orig>رئيس مجلس الوزراء</orig> and the Ministers <orig>الوزراء</orig> – each within their respective jurisdiction – shall implement this Decree-Law, and it shall come into effect from the date of its publication in the Official Gazette <orig>الجريدة الرسمية</orig>.

Amir of Kuwait <orig>أمير الكويت</orig>
Mishal Al-Ahmad Al-Jaber Al-Sabah <orig>مشعل الأحمد الجابر الصباح</orig>

Acting Prime Minister <orig>رئيس مجلس الوزراء بالنيابة</orig>
Fahad Yousef Saud Al-Sabah <orig>فهد يوسف سعود الصباح</orig>

Minister of Defense <orig>وزير الدفاع</orig>
Abdullah Ali Abdullah Al-Salem Al-Sabah <orig>عبد الله علي عبد الله السالم الصباح</orig>

## Explanatory Memorandum
### Regarding Decree-Law No. 61 of 2025 <orig>المرسوم بقانون رقم 61 لسنة 2025</orig> Extending the Period Stipulated in Law No. 3 of 2016 <orig>القانون رقم 3 لسنة 2016</orig> Authorizing the Government to Withdraw an Amount from the General Reserve Fund <orig>المال الاحتياطي العام</orig>

Law No. 3 of 2016 <orig>القانون رقم 3 لسنة 2016</orig> was issued, authorizing the Government to withdraw a specified sum from the General Reserve Fund <orig>الاحتياطي العام</orig> to enhance the state's defense capabilities over a period of ten fiscal years, commencing from the fiscal year 2015/2016, in order to keep pace with regional developments and ensure the readiness of the armed forces <orig>القوات المسلحة</orig>.
Given the approaching end of the period specified by the aforementioned Law, and the continued need to complete approved defense projects, it has become necessary to extend this period for an additional two fiscal years.
This extension aims to enable the competent authorities <orig>الجهات المختصة</orig> to complete armament and military equipment programs in accordance with pre-determined plans, without exceeding the amount specified in the aforementioned Law No. 3 of 2016 <orig>القانون رقم 3 لسنة 2016</orig>, as no amendment has been made to the allocated expenditure volume; rather, the extension is limited to granting more time to complete existing defense projects.
Provided that the Supreme Defense Council <orig>مجلس الدفاع الأعلى</orig> continues to exercise its powers as defined by the aforementioned Law No. 3 of 2016 <orig>القانون رقم 3 لسنة 2016</orig>, including supervising the allocation and disbursement of approved funds, and overseeing the implementation of contracts to ensure optimal use of financial resources and achievement of the prescribed defense objectives.
And since the Amiri Order <orig>الأمر الأميري</orig> was issued on 2 Dhu al-Qa'dah 1445 AH, corresponding to 10/5/2024 AD, including a provision in Article (4) thereof that laws shall be issued by decree-laws, the accompanying draft Decree-Law <orig>مشروع المرسوم بقانون</orig> has been prepared, consisting of two articles.
Where Article One of the draft stipulated the extension of the period provided for in Articles One and Two of the aforementioned Law No. 3 of 2016 <orig>القانون رقم 3 لسنة 2016</orig> for an additional two fiscal years, and Article Two of the draft obligated both the Prime Minister <orig>رئيس مجلس الوزراء</orig> and the Ministers <orig>الوزراء</orig> to implement it and act upon it from the date of its publication in the Official Gazette <orig>الجريدة الرسمية</orig>.

<footer>
Issued at Seif Palace <orig>قصر السيف</orig> on: 27 Ramadan 1446 AH
Corresponding to: 27 March 2025 AD
</footer>
<page_end>2</page_end>

# Decree No. 61 of 2025
## Amending Decree No. 139 of 2024
## Regarding Judicial Promotions and Transfers

- Having reviewed the Constitution,
- And Amiri Order <orig>الأمر الأميري</orig> issued on 2 Dhu al-Qi'dah 1445 AH corresponding to 10 May 2024 AD,
- And Decree-Law No. 14 of 1977 <orig>المرسوم بالقانون رقم 14 لسنة 1977</orig> concerning the grades and salaries of judges, members of the Public Prosecution <orig>النيابة العامة</orig>, and the Department of Fatwa and Legislation <orig>إدارة الفتوى والتشريع</orig>, and its amending laws,
- And the Law on the Organization of the Judiciary <orig>قانون تنظيم القضاء</orig> issued by Decree-Law No. 23 of 1990 <orig>المرسوم بالقانون رقم 23 لسنة 1990</orig> and its amending laws,
- And Decree No. 57 of 1990 <orig>المرسوم رقم 57 لسنة 1990</orig> concerning the salaries and allowances of judges, members of the Public Prosecution <orig>النيابة العامة</orig>, and the Department of Fatwa and Legislation <orig>إدارة الفتوى والتشريع</orig>, and its amending decrees,
- And Decree No. 108 of 2003 <orig>المرسوم رقم 108 لسنة 2003</orig> concerning the salaries and allowances of judges and members of the Public Prosecution <orig>النيابة العامة</orig>, amended by Decree No. 23 of 2004 <orig>المرسوم رقم 23 لسنة 2004</orig>,
- And Decree No. 41 of 2009 <orig>المرسوم رقم 41 لسنة 2009</orig> regarding the granting of a special judicial allowance to judges and members of the Public Prosecution <orig>النيابة العامة</orig>, and its amendments by Decree No. 162 of 2011 <orig>المرسوم رقم 162 لسنة 2011</orig> and Decree No. 126 of 2018 <orig>المرسوم رقم 126 لسنة 2018</orig>,
- And Decree No. 84 of 2024 <orig>المرسوم رقم 84 لسنة 2024</orig> concerning Ministerial Substitutions and Delegations <orig>الحلول والإنابات الوزارية</orig>, and its amending decrees,
- And Decree No. 139 of 2024 <orig>المرسوم رقم 139 لسنة 2024</orig> regarding judicial promotions and transfers,
- And after the approval of the Supreme Judicial Council <orig>المجلس الأعلى للقضاء</orig> at its session No. (2024/29) held on 17/9/2024,
- And based on the submission of the Minister of Justice <orig>وزير العدل</orig>,
- And after the approval of the Council of Ministers <orig>مجلس الوزراء</orig>,
We have decreed the following:
### Article One
The order of names listed in Article One of Decree No. 139 of 2024 <orig>المرسوم رقم 139 لسنة 2024</orig> regarding judicial promotions and transfers shall be amended as follows:

Renewal of the license for a collective investment scheme for Boubyan Multi-Asset Holding Fund <orig>صندوق بوبيان متعدد الأصول القابض</orig>, for a period of three years, renewable, effective from 2025/04/25.

# Capital Markets Authority <orig>هيئة أسواق المال</orig>
## Resolution No. (54) of 2025
Regarding the Exemption of Insurance Products from Collective Investment Schemes

**Having reviewed:**
- Law No. (7) of 2010 regarding the Establishment of the Capital Markets Authority <orig>هيئة أسواق المال</orig> and the Regulation of Securities Activities, and its Executive Regulations and amendments;
- And the Board of Commissioners of the Capital Markets Authority <orig>هيئة أسواق المال</orig> Resolution No. (B.C.C.M.A.-9 of 2025) issued at its meeting No. (9) of 2025 held on 2025/03/26.

**Decided the following:**
### Article One:
Article (1-1-2) of Book Thirteen (Collective Investment Schemes) <orig>أنظمة الاستثمار الجماعي</orig> of the Executive Regulations of Law No. (7) of 2010 regarding the Establishment of the Capital Markets Authority <orig>هيئة أسواق المال</orig> and the Regulation of Securities Activities and their amendments, shall be amended as set forth in Attachment No. (1) to this Resolution.

### Article Two:
The competent authorities shall implement this Resolution, each within its jurisdiction, and it shall be effective from the date of its issuance and published in the Official Gazette.

Acting Executive Director
Othman Ibrahim Al-Essa <orig>عثمان إبراهيم العيسى</orig>

<table_caption>Attachment No. 1: Amendment to Article 1-1-2 of Book Thirteen (Collective Investment Schemes)</table_caption>
<table>
| No. | Book | Chapter | Article | Type of Amendment | Text Before Amendment | Text After Amendment |
|:--|:-------|:-------|:-------|:---|:---|:---|
| 1 | Thirteen | One | 1-1-2 | Amendment of Article | The following are not included in collective investment schemes: 1. Insurance contracts and related investment instruments, and investments managed as part of Takaful insurance contracts. 2. Investment accounts with Islamic banks subject to the supervision of the Central Bank. 3. Investment portfolios. 4. Contracts concluded between companies belonging to the same group. 5. Savings, pension, retirement, or benefit schemes established for the benefit of company employees. 6. Any other cases that the Authority decides to exclude from the scope of collective investment schemes. | The following are not included in collective investment schemes: 1. Insurance products whose purpose is to pay specific amounts due to death, disability, reaching a certain age, abandonment, or upon the expiry of the agreed term, or life insurance, without the investment results being connected to profit or loss. 2. Investment accounts subject to the supervision of the Central Bank. 3. Investment portfolios. 4. Contracts concluded between companies belonging to the same group. 5. Savings, pension, retirement, or benefit schemes established for the benefit of company employees. 6. Any other cases that the Authority decides to exclude from the scope of collective investment schemes. |
</table>

Issued on: April 2, 2025 AD

<table_caption>Annex No. (1) - Amendments to the Executive Regulations of the Capital Markets Authority Law</table_caption>
<table>
| No. | Book | Article No. | Type of Amendment | Article After Amendment | Article Before Amendment |
|:--|:-------|:---|:---|:---|:---|
| 1. | Two | 1-2-6      | Article Amendment | A committee for receiving complaints and grievances shall be formed by a decision of the Board, consisting of no more than four members with expertise in financial, economic, and legal affairs, including a chairman and a vice-chairman of the committee. The committee shall receive complaints from any interested party regarding any error committed by any licensed person or entity subject to the Authority's supervision, and it shall also receive grievances regarding decisions issued by the Authority. The committee's deliberations shall be confidential, and its decisions shall be issued by majority vote; if votes are tied, the side with the chairman shall prevail. One of the Authority's employees specializing in any of the aforementioned specializations may also be selected as a member of this formation. | A committee for receiving complaints and grievances shall be formed by a decision of the Board, consisting of no more than four members with expertise in financial, economic, and legal affairs, including a chairman and a vice-chairman of the committee, for a period of two years renewable once. The committee shall receive complaints from any interested party regarding any error committed by any licensed person or entity subject to the Authority's supervision, and it shall also receive grievances regarding decisions issued by the Authority. The committee's deliberations shall be confidential, and its decisions shall be issued by majority vote; if votes are tied, the side with the chairman shall prevail. |
</table>

{
  "page_title": "Decision No. (56) for the year 2025 regarding a special marketing license for a collective investment scheme established outside the State of Kuwait granted to Kuwait Financial Centre for marketing shares of MKZ Development 46 <orig>قرار رقم (56) لسنة 2025 بشأن رخصة تسويق خاص لنظام استثمار جماعي مؤسس خارج دولة الكويت ممنوحة لشركة المركز المالي الكويتي لتسويق أسهم شركة إم كي زي ديفيلوبمنت 46</orig>",
  "document_date": "2025-04-02",
  "issue_number": 1733,
  "volume_number": 71,
  "document_type": "decree",
  "languages_detected": ["ar", "en", "mixed"],
  "page_type": "content",
  "authors": "Ziyad Yaqoub Yousef Al-Fulaij <orig>زياد يعقوب يوسف الفليج</orig>",
  "publisher": "Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig>",
  "page_summary": "This page outlines Decision No. 56 for 2025, granting a special marketing license to Kuwait Financial Centre (Markaz) for marketing 35,000 shares of MKZ Development 46, detailing the terms, conditions, and responsibilities related to this collective investment scheme and its publication."
}
</page_metadata>
<header>
Kuwait Today / Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig> Issue No. 1733 Seventy-first Year Sunday, 8 Shawwal 1446 AH - 6/4/2025 AD
</header>

Decided the following:

## Article One

Kuwait Financial Centre Company <orig>شركة المركز المالي الكويتي</orig> is licensed to privately market 35,000 shares (only thirty-five thousand shares) of MKZ Development 46 Company <orig>شركة إم كي زي ديفيلوبمنت 46</orig>, established in the Cayman Islands, within the State of Kuwait <orig>دولة الكويت</orig>, and the offer price shall be 1,000 Euros (only one thousand Euros) per share.

## Article Two

The shares to be marketed within the State of Kuwait <orig>دولة الكويت</orig> shall be offered to professional clients only, as per the text stipulated in Book One (Definitions) of the Executive Regulations of Law No. 7 of 2010 regarding the Establishment of the Capital Markets Authority <orig>هيئة أسواق المال</orig> and the Regulation of Securities Activities and their amendments. The entity receiving subscription requests shall be:
- Kuwait Financial Centre Company <orig>شركة المركز المالي الكويتي</orig>.

## Article Three

The objectives of the collective investment scheme <orig>نظام الاستثمار الجماعي</orig> shall be determined based on what is stated in the prospectus.

## Article Four

The marketing license duration is one year, renewable annually, starting from the date of issuance of the Authority's <orig>الهيئة</orig> license certificate and after payment of the prescribed fees.

## Article Five

The prescribed fees shall be paid within one month from the date of issuance of this decision. In case of failure to pay the fees within the specified period, the decision shall be considered null and void.

## Article Six

The competent authorities <orig>الجهات المختصة</orig> shall implement this decision, each within its jurisdiction. It shall be effective from the date of its issuance and published in the Official Gazette <orig>الجريدة الرسمية</orig>.

Issued on: April 2, 2025 AD
Head of Supervision Sector
Ziad Yaqoub Yousef Al-Fulaij <orig>زياد يعقوب يوسف الفليج</orig>

<header>
Kuwait Today / Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig> Issue 1733, Seventy-First Year
9
Sunday, 8 Shawwal 1446 AH - 6/4/2025 AD

# Resolution No. (57) of 2025
## Regarding
## Amending Certain Provisions of the Executive Regulations of Law No. (7) of 2010
## Regarding the Establishment of the Capital Markets Authority <orig>هيئة أسواق المال</orig> and the Regulation of Securities Activities and their Amendments

Having reviewed:
- Law No. (7) of 2010 regarding the establishment of the Capital Markets Authority <orig>هيئة أسواق المال</orig> and the regulation of securities activities, its executive regulations, and their amendments;
- And on the two resolutions of the Board of Commissioners of the Capital Markets Authority <orig>مجلس مفوضي هيئة أسواق المال</orig> Nos. (B.C.CMA 9-9 of 2025 and B.C.CMA 11-9 of 2025) in its meeting No. (9) of 2025 held on 26/03/2025;

It has been decided as follows:

### Article One:
Appendix No. (4) regarding the schedule of Authority <orig>الهيئة</orig> service fees from Book Two (Capital Markets Authority <orig>هيئة أسواق المال</orig>) of the Executive Regulations of Law No. (7) of 2010 regarding the establishment of the Capital Markets Authority <orig>هيئة أسواق المال</orig> and the regulation of securities activities and their amendments shall be amended in accordance with Annex No. (1) of this Resolution.

### Article Two:
Book Three (Law Enforcement <orig>إنفاذ القانون</orig>) of the Executive Regulations of Law No. (7) of 2010 regarding the establishment of the Capital Markets Authority <orig>هيئة أسواق المال</orig> and the regulation of securities activities and their amendments shall be amended in accordance with Annex No. (2) of this Resolution.

### Article Three:
Book Five (Securities Activities and Registered Persons <orig>أنشطة الأوراق المالية و الأشخاص المسجلون</orig>) of the Executive Regulations of Law No. (7) of 2010 regarding the establishment of the Capital Markets Authority <orig>هيئة أسواق المال</orig> and the regulation of securities activities and their amendments shall be amended in accordance with Annex No. (3) of this Resolution.

### Article Four:
Both Appendix No. (7) "Application Form for Cancellation of Securities Activities <orig>نموذج طلب إلغاء أنشطة أوراق مالية</orig>", and (11) "Application Form for Approval of Effective Control over a Licensed Person <orig>نموذج طلب الموافقة على سيطرة فعلية على الشخص المرخص له</orig>" from Book Five (Securities Activities and Registered Persons <orig>أنشطة الأوراق المالية والأشخاص المسجلون</orig>) regarding the establishment of the Capital Markets Authority <orig>هيئة أسواق المال</orig> and the regulation of securities activities and their amendments shall be amended in accordance with Annex No. (4) of this Resolution.

### Article Five:
The competent authorities shall implement this Resolution, each within its jurisdiction, and it shall be effective from the date of its issuance and published in the Official Gazette <orig>الجريدة الرسمية</orig>.

<footer>
Issued on: 3 April 2025 AD
Acting Executive Director
Othman Ibrahim Al-Essa <orig>عثمان إبراهيم العيسى</orig>
</footer>
<page_end>9</page_end>

| | | - Category Three: | |

| 1-1-7 | Application for increasing the marketing share of collective investment scheme units established outside the State of Kuwait <orig>دولة الكويت</orig> during the marketing license period. | 100 K.D. (One Hundred Kuwaiti Dinars) | Upon submission of the application. |

| 1-1-8 | Application for establishment and licensing of a contractual collective investment scheme and licensing of the Special Purpose Vehicle <orig>الشركة ذات الغرض الخاص</orig> that issues its units. | 1,000 K.D. (One Thousand Kuwaiti Dinars) | Upon submission of the application. |

# 1-2 Listing and Delisting

<table_caption>Fees for Listing and Delisting of Shares</table_caption>
<table>

|:---|:---|:---|:---|
| 1-2-1 | Application for listing shares of Kuwaiti and non-Kuwaiti joint-stock companies on the Exchange. | 5,000 K.D. (Five Thousand Kuwaiti Dinars) | Upon submission of the listing application. |
| 1-2-2 | Application for listing shares of Kuwaiti joint-stock companies listed on non-Kuwaiti exchanges. | 2,000 K.D. (Two Thousand Kuwaiti Dinars) | Upon submission of the application. |
| 1-2-3 | Application for listing a Kuwaiti or non-Kuwaiti collective investment scheme on the Exchange. | 2,000 K.D. (Two Thousand Kuwaiti Dinars) | Upon submission of the application. |
| 1-2-4 | Application for voluntary delisting of shares of a listed company from the Exchange. | 5,000 K.D. (Five Thousand Kuwaiti Dinars) | Upon submission of the application. |
</table>

|:---|:---|:---|:---|

</table>

| 3-3 | Application for Partial Purchase Offer | 10,000 K.D. (Ten Thousand Kuwaiti Dinars) <orig>دينار كويتي</orig> | Upon submission of the partial purchase offer document to the Authority. One per mille (0.001) of the total transaction value, not less than 2,000 K.D. (Two Thousand Kuwaiti Dinars) <orig>دينار كويتي</orig> and not exceeding 250,000 K.D. (Two Hundred and Fifty Thousand Kuwaiti Dinars) <orig>دينار كويتي</orig>. Acquisition execution fees are distributed as follows: 1) Capital Markets Authority <orig>هيئة أسواق المال</orig> 60% 2) Securities Exchange <orig>بورصة الأوراق المالية</orig> 30% 3) Clearing Agency <orig>وكالة المقاصة</orig> 10%. Upon execution of the acquisition, no other entity is entitled to collect any other fees. |
| 3-4 | Fees for applying to execute division operations for companies subject to the Authority's supervision. | 10,000 K.D. (Ten Thousand Kuwaiti Dinars) <orig>دينار كويتي</orig> | Upon submission of the draft division contract to the Authority. Upon submitting an application to execute the division operation to the Authority. |
| 3-5 | Application for Exemption from Mandatory Acquisition Provisions if the applicant is a legal entity. | 4,000 K.D. (Four Thousand Kuwaiti Dinars) <orig>دينار كويتي</orig> | Payable upon submission of the application for exemption from mandatory acquisition provisions if the applicant is a legal entity. |
| 3-5 | Application for Exemption from Mandatory Acquisition Provisions if the applicant is a natural person. | 2,000 K.D. (Two Thousand Kuwaiti Dinars) <orig>دينار كويتي</orig> | Payable upon submission of the application for exemption from mandatory acquisition provisions if the applicant is a natural person. |
</table>

| 10-4 | Application for approval to add/delete an activity for a Special Purpose Vehicle <orig>الشركة ذات الغرض الخاص</orig> that issues units of a contractual collective investment scheme. | 100 K.D. (One Hundred Kuwaiti Dinars) <orig>دينار كويتي</orig> | Upon submission of the application |

| 1-13-4 | Application for resolution on the expiration of the collective investment scheme and appointment of a liquidator. | 500 K.D. (Five Hundred Kuwaiti Dinars) <orig>دينار كويتي</orig> | Upon submission of the application |
| 2-13-4 | Application for resolution on the expiration of the collective investment scheme before the expiry of the period specified in the contract or articles of association, upon the request of the collective investment scheme manager or one of the unitholders. | 1,000 K.D. (One Thousand Kuwaiti Dinars) <orig>دينار كويتي</orig> | Upon submission of the application |

11: Withdrawal of Service Request (Refund of Paid Fee):
11-1 Without prejudice to the provisions for withdrawing service requests and refunding fees stipulated in the table above, the submitted service request may be withdrawn and the paid fee partially refunded in accordance with the provisions mentioned below, for some services marked with (**) in the table above. Withdrawal and fee refund do not apply to other services.
11-2 The service applicant or their legal representative may withdraw the service request, based on a request submitted to the Authority <orig>الهيئة</orig> stating the reasons for withdrawal, and at the latest by the next business day following the day of submitting the service request.
11-3 The withdrawal request shall be decided upon within two business days of its submission, and the deadline for deciding on the request may be extended if the Authority <orig>الهيئة</orig> deems it necessary, provided that the commencement of examining the service matter has not occurred.
11-4 The paid fee shall be partially refunded if the Authority <orig>الهيئة</orig> approves the service withdrawal request, at a rate of 25% of the fee paid for some services listed in the fee schedule.

<page_metadata>
{
  "page_title": "Regulations and Procedures for Financial Activities",
  "document_date": "2025-04-06",
  "issue_number": 1733,
  "volume_number": 71,
  "document_type": "official_gazette",
  "languages_detected": ["ar"],
  "page_type": "content",
  "authors": null,
  "publisher": "State of Kuwait <orig>دولة الكويت</orig>",
  "page_summary": "This page from the official gazette details procedures for financial activities, including conditions for business operation, cancellation of licenses, and obtaining approval for actual control over licensed entities, along with a table of contents for related appendices."
}
</page_metadata>
<header>
Kuwait Today / Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig> Issue 1733, Seventy-First Year
Sunday, 8 Shawwal 1446 AH - 6 / 4 / 2025 AD
16
</header>

*   A declaration and undertaking by the Chairman of the Board of Directors or his deputy to adhere to the controls specified in the Law and this Regulation, and to prevent the licensed person from repeatedly committing violations, and any other undertakings specified by the Authority <orig>الهيئة</orig>.
*   Any other documents or information requested by the Authority <orig>الهيئة</orig> to ensure that the licensed person meets the essential conditions stipulated in Article (1-7) of this Book.
2. The Authority <orig>الهيئة</orig> shall decide on the resumption of the suspended or restricted activity of the licensed person within two months from the date of receiving the plan referred to in the previous item, provided that all required information and documents are complete.
3. The Authority <orig>الهيئة</orig> shall notify the licensed person of its decision to approve or reject the plan. In the event that the Authority <orig>الهيئة</orig> approves the plan, the Authority <orig>الهيئة</orig> shall issue a decision to allow the licensed person to resume the activity at the time or lift the restriction, after payment of the prescribed fees.

### Submission of Cancellation Application

The licensed person shall submit an application for license cancellation in accordance with the requirements of the Financial Securities Activities License Cancellation Form in Appendix No. (7) of this Book, attaching all required documents and information, provided that the documents include proof of notification to the Central Bank <orig>البنك المركزي</orig> for entities subject to its supervision.
The Authority <orig>الهيئة</orig> may request – at any time after receiving the application – any additional documents or information if it deems it necessary.
In the event that the licensed person fails to submit the required documents and data within the period specified by the Authority <orig>الهيئة</orig> without an acceptable excuse from the Authority <orig>الهيئة</orig>, the application shall be considered null and void.

### Submission of an Application to Obtain the Authority's Approval for Effective Control over the Licensed Person According to the Following Procedures:

1.  The application shall be submitted according to the form in Appendix No. (11) of this Book, along with the payment of the prescribed fees, at least sixty (60) days before entering into arrangements or agreements that lead to effective control over the licensed person. The period commences from the date of completion of all required data and information.
2.  The Authority <orig>الهيئة</orig> shall decide on the application within a maximum period of sixty (60) days from the date of its submission, provided it is complete with any information or documents requested by the Authority <orig>الهيئة</orig>. The Authority <orig>الهيئة</orig> shall grant its approval to the application after ensuring that any effective control over the licensed person or ownership of shares or capital stakes will not hinder the supervision and oversight of the licensed person or lead to non-compliance with the Law and this Regulation. This is after the applicant pays the prescribed fees. In case the Authority <orig>الهيئة</orig> rejects the application, the rejection decision must be reasoned.

<page_metadata>
{
  "page_title": "Instructions for License Cancellation <orig>تعليمات إلغاء الترخيص</orig>",
  "document_date": "2025-04-06",
  "issue_number": 1733,
  "volume_number": 71,
  "document_type": "official_gazette",
  "languages_detected": ["ar", "mixed"],
  "page_type": "content",
  "authors": null,
  "publisher": "Kuwait Today / Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig>",
  "page_summary": "This page outlines the instructions and procedures for cancelling a license, detailing requirements such as obtaining prior approval, submitting necessary documents, adhering to timelines, and providing contact information for the Capital Markets Authority."
}
</page_metadata>
<header>
Kuwait Today / Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig> Issue 1733, Seventy-First Year
17
Sunday, 8 Shawwal 1446 AH - 6/4/2025 AD
</header>
# 1. Instructions

*   The licensed person <orig>الشخص المرخص له</orig> shall fulfill all requirements stated in Appendix (27) <orig>الملحق (27)</orig> - Instructions for Requesting Cancellation of License for Some or All Securities Activities <orig>أنشطة أوراق مالية</orig> - before submitting a request for cancellation of the securities activities license.
*   Submitting a request for license cancellation requires prior approval from the Extraordinary General Assembly <orig>الجمعية العامة غير العادية</orig> on the proposal to cancel the license for some or all securities activities, provided that such cancellation is justified.
*   The licensed person <orig>الشخص المرخص له</orig> is obligated to submit the items stated in Book Five <orig>الكتاب الخامس</orig> concerning license cancellation upon the request of the licensed person.
*   The proposed cancellation date shall be at least six months after the date of submitting the application.
*   The Authority <orig>الهيئة</orig> may request any additional information or documents or any clarifications from the licensed person <orig>الشخص المرخص له</orig> during the review of their application. If the licensed person fails to provide the required documents and information within the period specified by the Authority <orig>الهيئة</orig> in the notification without an acceptable excuse from the Authority <orig>الهيئة</orig>, the application shall be considered null and void.
*   The Authority <orig>الهيئة</orig> shall decide on the application within two months of fulfilling all required documents and information.
*   Provide the Authority <orig>الهيئة</orig> with supporting documents for the application in case any requirement in this form or the required attachments does not apply to the applicant.
*   The applicant is obligated to comply with all procedures issued by the Authority <orig>الهيئة</orig> required after the decision on the submitted application.
*   Units subject to the supervision of the Central Bank <orig>البنك المركزي</orig> must adhere to the instructions regarding license cancellation as stipulated in the Memorandum of Understanding <orig>مذكرة التفاهم</orig> concluded between the Capital Markets Authority <orig>هيئة أسواق المال</orig> and the Central Bank <orig>البنك المركزي</orig>.
*   The licensed person <orig>الشخص المرخص له</orig> is obligated to notify the Authority <orig>الهيئة</orig> in writing immediately upon the occurrence of any impediments in the procedures for canceling the securities activities license.
*   The licensed person <orig>الشخص المرخص له</orig> is obligated to submit a license renewal application if they fail to comply with the specified timeframe for license cancellation.
*   The Authority <orig>الهيئة</orig> may oblige the applicant for license cancellation to take all measures and precautions that ensure no harm is caused to their interests or the integrity of the financial system as a result of the license cancellation.
*   The licensed person <orig>الشخص المرخص له</orig> may resort to the arbitration system <orig>نظام التحكيم</orig> at the Authority <orig>الهيئة</orig> to settle disputes related to securities activities.
*   The licensed person <orig>الشخص المرخص له</orig> must submit the cancellation request through the Authority's <orig>الهيئة</orig> electronic portal <orig>بوابة الهيئة الإلكترونية</orig> and pay the prescribed fees. In case of any inquiries regarding the application submission or related matters, contact the Licensing and Registration Department <orig>إدارة التراخيص والتسجيل</orig> at the Capital Markets Authority <orig>هيئة أسواق المال</orig> at this address:

Kuwait - Sharq - Al Hamra Tower <orig>برج الحمراء</orig>/20th Floor - Capital Markets Authority <orig>هيئة أسواق المال</orig>
P.O. Box 3913 Al Safat <orig>الصفوة</orig> 13040 Kuwait
lrd@cma.gov.kw

## Instructions
- Please complete this form in its entirety and ensure all attachments related to this form are included.
- This form is to be submitted by any entity wishing to enter into arrangements or agreements that lead to actual control over a licensed person in accordance with Article (1-19) of this Book.
- The applicant is obligated to pay the prescribed fees for the application for approval of actual control over a licensed person.
- Persons subject to the provisions of Book Nine (Mergers and Acquisitions) of these Regulations are exempt from completing this form.
- Prior approval from the Central Bank <orig>البنك المركزي</orig> must be obtained for units under its supervision.
- Compliance with the rules of the Stock Exchange <orig>البورصة</orig> and the rules for trading unlisted securities on Boursa Kuwait <orig>بورصة الكويت</orig> must be observed.
- This form must be submitted at least 60 days prior to the commencement date of the actual control procedures.
- The Authority <orig>الهيئة</orig> may request any additional information, documents, or clarifications from the applicant when reviewing the application.
- The applicant must send this form or any inquiries regarding its completion or related matters to the Licensing and Registration Department <orig>إدارة التراخيص والتسجيل</orig> at the Capital Markets Authority <orig>هيئة أسواق المال</orig> at this address:
Kuwait - Sharq - Al Hamra Tower <orig>برج الحمراء</orig> / 15th Floor - Capital Markets Authority <orig>هيئة أسواق المال</orig>
P.O. Box 3913 Safat 13040 Kuwait
lrd@cma.gov.kw

### 4. Acknowledgment / Declaration <orig>إقرار</orig>
*   I acknowledge my awareness of the obligations stipulated in Capital Markets Authority Law No. 7 of 2010 <orig>قانون هيئة أسواق المال رقم 7 لسنة 2010</orig>, its Executive Regulations <orig>اللائحة التنفيذية</orig> and their amendments, and the regulations, decisions, and instructions issued by the Capital Markets Authority <orig>هيئة أسواق المال</orig>.
*   I affirm the accuracy, completeness, and truthfulness of the information provided in this form and its associated attachments, and the accuracy of the facts stated. I also acknowledge my knowledge of the laws and regulations of the Capital Markets Authority <orig>هيئة أسواق المال</orig> concerning penalties resulting from providing any incorrect or misleading information in this form or its associated attachments.
*   I acknowledge that I must inform the Capital Markets Authority <orig>هيئة أسواق المال</orig> of any changes that may occur to the information and data provided to the Authority concerning this form.
*   I acknowledge my awareness of the right of the Capital Markets Authority <orig>هيئة أسواق المال</orig> to take any punitive or disciplinary action against any person who provides incorrect or misleading data or declarations in this form.
    This is my acknowledgment and undertaking thereof.

## Announcement

The owners of the company / Herbal Mobile Food Sales Company <orig>شركة عشبية لبيع الأغذية المتنقلة</orig> ## Company Under Liquidation <orig>الشركة تحت التصفية</orig>
have submitted a request to the Department of Partnerships <orig>إدارة شركات الأشخاص</orig> at the Ministry <orig>الوزارة</orig> to carry out/
Dissolution and Liquidation of the Company <orig>حل وتصفية الشركة</orig>
Legal Entity:
Anyone with an objection is requested to submit it to the General Court <orig>المحكمة الكلية</orig> within thirty days from the date of publication of this announcement, in accordance with the usual procedures for filing a lawsuit. The submission of an objection shall result in the continued obligation of the joint partners <orig>الشركاء المتضامنين</orig> in the case of a general partnership <orig>التضامنية</orig> or simple limited partnership <orig>التوصية البسيطة</orig> only in the face of this creditor, until a final judgment is rendered on their objection.

## Announcement

Messrs. / Miska Company for Trading in All Medical Equipment and Supplies <orig>شركة مسكا للتجارة في جميع المعدات والمستلزمات الطبية</orig>
have submitted an agency registration request to the Commercial Register Department <orig>إدارة السجل التجاري</orig> approved by the Ministry <orig>الوزارة</orig>, where the agency is registered under registration number: 2025/00260
Company and Nationality: Planner - United Kingdom
The agency's activity consists of: Incubators (excluding BT37 for human
Sunday, 8 Shawwal 1446 AH - 2025/4/6 AD
</header>
23
in vitro fertilization <orig>الأنابيب البشرية</orig>), controlled-rate freezers, deep cryogenic storage, cooling, and transport vessels for materials, monitoring systems, tracking systems, CELL-TEK <orig>سيل-تك</orig> chambers, ZANDAIR <orig>زانداير</orig> devices.

*   The practice/tender document can be obtained starting from Sunday, 2025/3/30, and on subsequent days during official working hours of the Financial Affairs Department (Ministry Building located in Al-Riqqa <orig>الرقعي</orig> area - 6th Floor - Tenders Department). The last deadline for submitting bids is Sunday, 2025/4/20, at noon. Bids received after this deadline will not be considered, noting that the mentioned fees are non-refundable.
*   All documents must be submitted on a non-copyable CD, except for the bid form and initial security, which must be submitted as hard copies.
*   Bids must be placed in the tenders box at the Tenders Department, along with an initial security deposit of (750 K.D. <orig>د.ك</orig>) in the form of a letter of guarantee or a certified check approved by one of the accredited local banks in the State of Kuwait <orig>دولة الكويت</orig>, unconditional and free of any reservations, and it must be valid throughout the bid validity period, which is (90 days).
*   All companies participating in the practice/tender are invited to attend the opening of envelopes at the date and place specified in the table above.
Note:
The practice/tender document can be withdrawn by specialized companies in this field, provided they are registered with the Ministry's Tenders Department, from 9:00 AM to 1:00 PM, with the submission of the 2025 registration card.
Ministry's Electronic Tenders Website:
(https://tenders.awqaf.gov.kw/Tender/Tender_Public_Practice)

# Ministry of Commerce and Industry <orig>وزارة التجارة والصناعة</orig>
Announcement
The owners of Axelland Wholesale Company for Perfumes, Cosmetics, and Cosmetic Soap <orig>أكسيلند للبيع بالجملة للعطور ومستحضرات التجميل وصابون التجميل</orig> ##Company Under Liquidation
Request to the Department of Partnership Companies at the Ministry to carry out/
Dissolution and Liquidation of the Company
Legal Entity: Limited Liability Company
Anyone with an objection is requested to submit it to the General Court <orig>المحكمة الكلية</orig> within thirty days from the date of publication of this announcement, in accordance with the usual procedures for filing a lawsuit. The submission of an objection shall result in the continued obligation of the joint partners, in the case of a general partnership or simple limited partnership, only in facing this creditor, until a judicial ruling is issued on their objection.

### Announcement
The owners of Al-Bustan Fruit for Vegetables and Fruits <orig>البستان فروت للخضار والفواكه</orig> ## Company Under Liquidation have submitted a request:
to the Department of Partnerships at the Ministry to carry out:
Dissolution and Liquidation of the Company
Legal Entity: One-Person Company
Anyone with an objection is requested to submit it to the General Court within thirty days from the date of publication of this announcement, in accordance with the usual procedures for filing a lawsuit. The submission of an objection shall result in the continued obligation of the joint partners, in the case of a general partnership or a simple limited partnership only, towards this creditor until their objection is decided by a judicial ruling.

Legal Entity / Sole Proprietorship Company
Anyone with an objection is requested to submit it to the General Court <orig>المحكمة الكلية</orig> within thirty days from the date of publication of this announcement, in accordance with the usual procedures for filing a lawsuit. The submission of an objection shall result in the continued obligation of the joint partners, in the case of a general partnership or a simple limited partnership, only in the face of this creditor until their objection is decided by a judicial ruling.

Legal Entity: One-Person Company
Anyone with an objection is requested to submit it to the General Court <orig>المحكمة الكلية</orig> within thirty days from the date of publication of this announcement, in accordance with the usual procedures for filing a lawsuit. The submission of an objection shall result in the continued obligation of the joint partners <orig>الشركاء المتضامنين</orig> in the case of a general partnership <orig>التضامنية</orig> or a simple limited partnership <orig>التوصية البسيطة</orig> only in the face of this creditor, until a final judgment is rendered on their objection.

<header>
Kuwait Today / Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig> Issue 1733 Seventy-First Year
Sunday, 8 Shawwal 1446 AH - 6/4/2025 AD
34
</header>


# Announcement
The following individuals have submitted:
<table_caption>Details of Individuals Associated with the Announcement</table_caption>
<table>
| Civil ID Number | Name | Capacity | Nationality |
|:---|:---|:-------|:--------|
| 259102600325 | Adel Salem Ali Mohammed <orig>عادل سالم علي محمد</orig> | Partner | Kuwait |
| 271040900024 | Youssef Abdel Moneim Hasabo Khodeir <orig>يوسف عبد المنعم حسبو خضير</orig> | Manager | Egypt |
| 248120200612 | Shahah Mohammed Fahad Al-Mudahi <orig>شاهه محمد فهد المضحي</orig> | Partner | Kuwait |
</table>

# Announcement
It is requested from the Companies Department <orig>إدارة شركات</orig> of this Ministry <orig>الوزارة</orig>:
To convert the individual license issued under number: 2000/707
dated 22/11/2022
Under the trade name: Nile Stars Men's Salon <orig>صالون نجوم النيل للرجال</orig>
and convert it into a Limited Liability Company <orig>شركة ذات مسئولية محدودة</orig>
Anyone with an objection is requested to submit a written objection to the aforementioned Department <orig>الإدارة المذكورة</orig> within fifteen days from the date of publication of this announcement, accompanied by proof of indebtedness, otherwise it will not be taken into consideration.

# Announcement
The owners of the company: Sada Al-Abrar General Trading Company <orig>صدى الابرار للتجارة العامة</orig> ## Company Under Liquidation <orig>الشركة تحت التصفية</orig> have submitted:
It is requested from the Partnerships Department <orig>إدارة شركات الأشخاص</orig> of the Ministry <orig>الوزارة</orig> for the procedure of: Dissolution and Liquidation of the Company <orig>حل وتصفية الشركة</orig>
Legal Entity: Limited Liability Company <orig>شركة ذات مسئولية محدودة</orig>
Anyone with an objection is requested to submit it to the General Court <orig>المحكمة الكلية</orig> within thirty days from the date of publication of this announcement, in accordance with the usual procedures for filing a lawsuit. The submission of an objection shall result in the continued obligation of the joint partners <orig>الشركاء المتضامنين</orig> in the case of a general partnership <orig>التضامنية</orig> or simple limited partnership <orig>التوصية البسيطة</orig> only in the face of this creditor, until a judicial ruling is issued on their objection.

  "page_summary": "This page contains multiple official announcements regarding the dissolution and liquidation of various companies in Kuwait, detailing the legal procedures for creditors to object to the liquidation process within a specified timeframe."

<header>
Kuwait Today / Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig> Issue 1733, Seventy-First Year 35
Sunday, 8 Shawwal 1446 AH - 6/4/2025 AD
</header>
Dissolution and Liquidation of the Company
Legal Entity
Simple Partnership <orig>شركة توصية بسيطة</orig>
Anyone with an objection is requested to submit it to the General Court <orig>المحكمة الكلية</orig> within thirty days from the date of publication of this announcement, in accordance with the usual procedures for filing a lawsuit. The submission of an objection shall result in the continued obligation of the joint partners <orig>الشركاء المتضامنين</orig> in the case of a general partnership <orig>التضامنية</orig> or a simple partnership <orig>التوصية البسيطة</orig> only, vis-à-vis this creditor, until a final judgment is rendered on their objection.

---

## Announcement
The owners of the company: Kuksel for Building Construction and Insulation Materials Contracting <orig>كوكسل لتشييد المباني ومقاولات المواد العازلة</orig> ##
The Company under Liquidation
A request has been submitted to the Department of Personal Companies <orig>إدارة شركات الأشخاص</orig> at the Ministry <orig>الوزارة</orig> to carry out:
Dissolution and Liquidation of the Company
Legal Entity
Limited Liability Company (LLC) <orig>شركة ذات مسؤولية محدودة</orig>
Anyone with an objection is requested to submit it to the General Court <orig>المحكمة الكلية</orig> within thirty days from the date of publication of this announcement, in accordance with the usual procedures for filing a lawsuit. The submission of an objection shall result in the continued obligation of the joint partners <orig>الشركاء المتضامنين</orig> in the case of a general partnership <orig>التضامنية</orig> or a simple partnership <orig>التوصية البسيطة</orig> only, vis-à-vis this creditor, until a final judgment is rendered on their objection.

---

<header>
Kuwait Today / Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig> Issue 1733, Seventy-First Year
Sunday, 8 Shawwal 1446 AH - 6/4/2025 AD
36
</header>
### Announcement

Legal Entity / One-Person Company <orig>شركة الشخص الواحد</orig>

Anyone with an objection is requested to submit it to the General Court <orig>المحكمة الكلية</orig> within thirty days from the date of publication of this announcement, in accordance with the usual procedures for filing a lawsuit. The submission of an objection shall result in the continued obligation of the joint partners <orig>الشركاء المتضامنين</orig> in the case of a general partnership <orig>التضامنية</orig> or simple limited partnership <orig>التوصية البسيطة</orig> only, in the face of this creditor, until a final judgment is rendered on their objection.

### Announcement

Mr. <orig>السيد</orig>: has applied.

<table_caption>Details of Individuals for License Conversion</table_caption>
<table>
| Civil ID Number | Name | Capacity / Role | Nationality |
|:---|:---|:-------|:--------|
| 252020200879 | Rahab Abbas Mohammed Sharif <orig>رحب عباس محمد شريف</orig> | Partner- | Kuwait |
| 272072500847 | Mehrdad Khalil Gholami <orig>مهرداد خليل غلامی</orig> | Manager | Iran |
</table>

Requests the Companies Department <orig>إدارة الشركات</orig> at this Ministry:
To convert the individual license issued under number: 2010/1460
- Dated 9/2/2022
Under the trade name: Sharif Exchange Establishment <orig>مؤسسه شريف للصيرفة</orig>
And convert it to a One-Person Company <orig>شركة الشخص الواحد</orig>
Anyone with an objection is requested to submit a written objection to the aforementioned department within fifteen days from the date of publication of this announcement, accompanied by a debt instrument <orig>سند المديونية</orig>, otherwise it will not be taken into consideration.

Anyone with an objection is requested to submit it to the General Court <orig>المحكمة الكلية</orig> within thirty days from the date of publication of this announcement, in accordance with the usual procedures for filing a lawsuit. The submission of an objection shall result in the continued obligation of the joint partners <orig>الشركاء المتضامنين</orig> in the case of a general partnership <orig>التضامنية</orig> or simple limited partnership <orig>التوصية البسيطة</orig> only, in the face of this creditor, until a final judgment is rendered on their objection.

<header>
37
Sunday, 8 Shawwal 1446 AH - 6/4/2025 AD
Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig> No. 1733, Seventy-First Year
</header>
## Dissolution and Liquidation of the Company
### Legal Entity
### One-Person Company
Anyone with an objection is requested to submit it to the General Court <orig>المحكمة الكلية</orig> within thirty days from the date of publication of this announcement, in accordance with the usual procedures for filing a lawsuit. The submission of an objection shall result in the continued obligation of the joint partners, in the case of a general partnership or a simple limited partnership only, towards this creditor until a final judgment is rendered on their objection.

## Announcement
The esteemed owners of Shinar for Trading Medicines, Equipment, Devices, and Medical Supplies <orig>شينار للإتجار بالأدوية والمعدات والأجهزة والمستلزمات الطبية</orig> Company under Liquidation, submitted a request to the Department of Partnerships <orig>إدارة شركات الأشخاص</orig> at the Ministry <orig>الوزارة</orig> to carry out: Dissolution and Liquidation of the Company.
### Legal Entity
### Limited Liability Company
Anyone with an objection is requested to submit it to the General Court <orig>المحكمة الكلية</orig> within thirty days from the date of publication of this announcement, in accordance with the usual procedures for filing a lawsuit. The submission of an objection shall result in the continued obligation of the joint partners, in the case of a general partnership or a simple limited partnership only, towards this creditor until a final judgment is rendered on their objection.

## Announcement
The esteemed owners of Pecan Corner for Sweets, Pies, and Pastries <orig>بيكان كورنر للحلويات والفطائر والمعجنات</orig> Company under Liquidation, submitted a request to the Department of Partnerships <orig>إدارة شركات الأشخاص</orig> at the Ministry <orig>الوزارة</orig> to carry out:
### Dissolution and Liquidation of the Company
### Legal Entity
### One-Person Company
Anyone with an objection is requested to submit it to the General Court <orig>المحكمة الكلية</orig> within thirty days from the date of publication of this announcement, in accordance with the usual procedures for filing a lawsuit. The submission of an objection shall result in the continued obligation of the joint partners, in the case of a general partnership or a simple limited partnership only, towards this creditor until a final judgment is rendered on their objection.

The esteemed owners of High Performance General Trading <orig>الأداء العالي للتجارة العامة</orig> Company under Liquidation, submitted a request to the Department of Partnerships <orig>إدارة شركات الأشخاص</orig> at the Ministry <orig>الوزارة</orig> to carry out:

The submission of an objection shall result in the continued obligation of the joint partners, in the case of a general partnership or a simple limited partnership only, towards this creditor until a final judgment is rendered on their objection.

Any person with an objection is requested to submit it to the General Court <orig>المحكمة الكلية</orig> within thirty days from the date of publication of this announcement, in accordance with the usual procedures for filing a lawsuit. The submission of an objection shall result in the continued obligation of the joint partners <orig>الشركاء المتضامنين</orig> in the case of a general partnership <orig>التضامنية</orig> or a simple limited partnership <orig>التوصية البسيطة</orig> only, in the face of this creditor, until a final judgment is rendered on their objection.

## Announcement

A request has been submitted to the Department of Partnerships <orig>إدارة شركات الأشخاص</orig> at the Ministry to carry out / dissolve and liquidate the company.

Legal Entity: One-Person Company <orig>شركة الشخص الواحد</orig>

Anyone with an objection is requested to submit it to the General Court <orig>المحكمة الكلية</orig> within thirty days from the date of publication of this announcement, in accordance with the usual procedures for filing a lawsuit. The submission of an objection shall result in the continued obligation of the joint partners <orig>الشركاء المتضامنين</orig> in the case of a general partnership <orig>التضامنية</orig> or simple limited partnership <orig>التوصية البسيطة</orig> only, in the face of this creditor, until a final judgment is rendered on their objection.

Dissolution and Liquidation of the Company
Legal Entity: One-Person Company <orig>شركة الشخص الواحد</orig>
Anyone with an objection is requested to submit it to the General Court <orig>المحكمة الكلية</orig> within thirty days from the date of publication of this announcement, in accordance with the usual procedures for filing a lawsuit. The submission of an objection shall result in the continued obligation of the joint partners <orig>الشركاء المتضامنين</orig> in the case of a general partnership <orig>التضامنية</orig> or simple limited partnership <orig>التوصية البسيطة</orig> only in the face of this creditor, until a judicial ruling is issued on their objection.

KWD 178,854,730.800 (One hundred seventy-eight million, eight hundred fifty-four thousand, seven hundred thirty Kuwaiti Dinars and 800 fils) by issuing 85,168,919 new shares (Eighty-five million, one hundred sixty-eight thousand, nine hundred nineteen shares) to be distributed as free bonus shares to eligible shareholders as specified in the timeline approved by the Ordinary General Assembly <orig>الجمعية العامة العادية</orig>, and covering the value of the resulting increase in the issued and paid-up capital in the amount of KWD 8,516,891.900 (Eight million, five hundred sixteen thousand, eight hundred ninety-one Kuwaiti Dinars and 900 fils) from the profit and loss account, and authorizing the Board of Directors <orig>مجلس الإدارة</orig> to dispose of fractional shares arising therefrom as it deems appropriate.

2- The amendment of Article No. (6) of the Articles of Association <orig>عقد التأسيس</orig> and Article No. (5) of the Bylaws <orig>النظام الأساسي</orig> was approved as follows:

**Text before amendment:**
The authorized, issued, and fully paid-up capital of the Bank was set at KWD 170,337,838.900 (One hundred seventy million, three hundred thirty-seven thousand, eight hundred thirty-eight Kuwaiti Dinars and 900 fils), divided into 1,703,378,389 shares (One billion, seven hundred three million, three hundred seventy-eight thousand, three hundred eighty-nine shares), with a nominal value of 100 fils (One hundred fils) per share, and all shares are cash shares.

**Text after amendment:**
The authorized, issued, and fully paid-up capital of the Bank was set at KWD 178,854,730.800 (One hundred seventy-eight million, eight hundred fifty-four thousand, seven hundred thirty Kuwaiti Dinars and 800 fils), divided into 1,788,547,308 shares (One billion, seven hundred eighty-eight million, five hundred forty-seven thousand, three hundred eight shares), with a nominal value of 100 fils (One hundred fils) per share, and all shares are cash shares.
Shareholders representing 3.036% of the attendance abstained.
Thus, the Extraordinary General Assembly <orig>الجمعية العامة غير العادية</orig> concluded its review of the topics on its agenda, and then Mr./ Chairman of the Assembly <orig>رئيس الجمعية</orig> announced the end of its meeting at 12:30 PM.

---

National Investment Company K.S.C. (Closed) <orig>شركة الوطني للاستثمار ش.م.ك (مقفلة)</orig>, and National Financial Brokerage Company K.S.C. (Closed) <orig>شركة الوطني للوساطة المالية ش.م.ك (مقفلة)</orig>, such that National Investment Company <orig>شركة الوطني للاستثمار</orig> is the merging company and National Financial Brokerage Company <orig>شركة الوطني للوساطة المالية</orig> is the merged company, and all its annexes, including the consultation of the independent investment advisor and the asset valuation report prepared by the independent asset valuer and the share exchange ratio, after obtaining the approvals of the relevant regulatory authorities <orig>الجهات الرقابية</orig>.

**Item Two:**
The merger by absorption between National Investment Company K.S.C. (Closed) <orig>شركة الوطني للاستثمار ش.م.ك (مقفلة)</orig> and National Financial Brokerage Company K.S.C. (Closed) <orig>شركة الوطني للوساطة المالية ش.م.ك (مقفلة)</orig> was approved, such that National Investment Company <orig>شركة الوطني للاستثمار</orig> is the merging company and National Financial Brokerage Company <orig>شركة الوطني للوساطة المالية</orig> is the merged company, through the dissolution of the merged company, in accordance with the provisions of Law No. (7) of 2010 <orig>القانون رقم (7) لسنة 2010</orig> and its executive regulations <orig>لائحته التنفيذية</orig>, and their amendments, after obtaining the approvals of the relevant regulatory authorities <orig>الجهات الرقابية</orig>.

**Item Three:**
The dissolution of National Financial Brokerage Company K.S.C. (Closed) <orig>شركة الوطني للوساطة المالية ش.م.ك (مقفلة)</orig> and the transfer of its financial liability by absorption (assets and liabilities), including all its assets, rights, and obligations, to National Investment Company K.S.C. (Closed) <orig>شركة الوطني للاستثمار ش.م.ك (مقفلة)</orig> was approved, and consequently, the termination of the legal personality of National Financial Brokerage Company <orig>شركة الوطني للوساطة المالية</orig> upon completion of the merger procedures, its delisting, and the cancellation of its licenses from the records of the Joint Stock Companies Department at the Ministry of Commerce and Industry <orig>وزارة التجارة والصناعة</orig>, in accordance with the provisions of Law No. (7) of 2010 <orig>القانون رقم (7) لسنة 2010</orig> regarding the establishment of the Capital Markets Authority <orig>هيئة أسواق المال</orig> and the regulation of securities activities and its executive regulations <orig>لائحته التنفيذية</orig>, and their amendments, and Law No. (1) of 2016 <orig>القانون رقم (1) لسنة 2016</orig> issuing the Companies Law and its executive regulations <orig>لائحته التنفيذية</orig>, and their amendments.
Accordingly, Mr. Tariq Abdul Latif Al-Shehab <orig>طارق عبد اللطيف الشهاب</orig> – Chairman of the Board of Directors <orig>رئيس مجلس الإدارة</orig> announced the end of the meeting at 12:30 PM.

Chairman of the Board of Directors <orig>رئيس مجلس الإدارة</orig>

Sunday, 8 Shawwal 1446 AH – 2025/4/6 CE

(K.S.C.) Public
Minutes of the Extraordinary General Assembly Meeting
Dated 2025/3/25
At exactly 12:45 PM on Tuesday, 2025/3/25, the Extraordinary General Assembly Meeting was held at the Company's head office. After the legal quorum was met with the attendance of shareholders owning and representing [191,944,794] shares out of the Company's total shares of [220,500,000] shares, i.e., 87.049%, and after reviewing the agenda, the following was approved:
1- Approval of increasing the Company's issued and paid-up capital from K.D. 22,050,000 <orig>دينار كويتي</orig> to K.D. 23,600,000 <orig>دينار كويتي</orig>, by issuing 15,500,000 shares equivalent to K.D. 1,550,000 <orig>دينار كويتي</orig> at a value of (100) Fils <orig>فلس</orig> per share, representing 7.029478%. These shares shall be distributed as free bonus shares to shareholders registered in the Company's books as of the end of the record date according to the timeline in the share entitlements disclosure form, and authorizing the Board of Directors <orig>مجلس الإدارة</orig> to dispose of fractional shares arising from the distribution of bonus shares as it deems appropriate.
2- Approval of amending Article (6) of the Articles of Incorporation <orig>عقد التأسيس</orig> and Article (7) of the Articles of Association <orig>النظام الأساسي</orig> as follows:
Text before amendment:
The Company's authorized capital is set at K.D. 30,000,000 <orig>دينار كويتي</orig> (Thirty Million Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig>) distributed over 300,000,000 shares, with each share valued at (100) Fils <orig>فلس</orig>, and all shares are cash shares. The Company's issued and paid-up capital is set at K.D. 22,050,000 <orig>دينار كويتي</orig> (Twenty-Two Million and Fifty Thousand Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig>) distributed over 220,500,000 shares, with each share valued at (100) Fils <orig>فلس</orig>, and all shares are cash shares.
Text after amendment:
The Company's authorized capital is set at K.D. 30,000,000 <orig>دينار كويتي</orig> (Thirty Million Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig>) distributed over 300,000,000 shares, with each share valued at (100) Fils <orig>فلس</orig>, and all shares are cash shares. The Company's issued and paid-up capital is set at K.D. 23,600,000 <orig>دينار كويتي</orig> (Twenty-Three Million and Six Hundred Thousand Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig>) distributed over 236,000,000 shares, with each share valued at (100) Fils <orig>فلس</orig>, and all shares are cash shares.
And after the approval of the competent regulatory authorities.
The meeting concluded at 1:00 PM.

Chairman of the Board of Directors <orig>رئيس مجلس الإدارة</orig>

Then proceeded to discuss the following agenda item:
*   Addition of a new clause to Article No. 47 of the Company's Articles of Association <orig>النظام الأساسي</orig>, to read as follows:
    *   Text of Article 47 before amendment:
        *   First: (10%) ten percent shall be deducted and allocated to the voluntary reserve <orig>الاحتياطي الاختياري</orig> account. The General Assembly <orig>الجمعية العامة</orig> may stop the deduction if the reserve exceeds half of the Company's capital.
        *   Second: (1%) one percent shall be deducted and allocated to the Kuwait Foundation for the Advancement of Sciences <orig>مؤسسة الكويت للتقدم العلمي</orig> account.
        *   Third: A percentage shall be deducted and allocated to the voluntary reserve <orig>الاحتياطي الاختياري</orig> account, as proposed by the Board of Directors <orig>مجلس الإدارة</orig> and approved by the General Assembly <orig>الجمعية العامة</orig>. This deduction shall be stopped by a resolution of the Ordinary General Assembly <orig>الجمعية العامة العادية</orig> based on a proposal from the Board of Directors <orig>مجلس الإدارة</orig>.
        *   Fourth: A portion of the profits shall be deducted based on a proposal from the Board of Directors <orig>مجلس الإدارة</orig> and its report to the General Assembly <orig>الجمعية العامة</orig> to meet the Company's obligations under labor laws <orig>قوانين العمل</orig>. These funds may not be distributed to shareholders.
        *   Fifth: The amount necessary for distributing an initial dividend <orig>حصة أولى من الأرباح</orig> of (5%) five percent to shareholders shall be deducted, as determined by the Board of Directors <orig>مجلس الإدارة</orig> and approved by the General Assembly <orig>الجمعية العامة</orig>.
    *   Text of Article 47 after amendment:
        *   First: (10%) ten percent shall be deducted and allocated to the voluntary reserve <orig>الاحتياطي الاختياري</orig> account. The General Assembly <orig>الجمعية العامة</orig> may stop the deduction if the reserve exceeds half of the Company's capital.
        *   Second: (1%) one percent shall be deducted and allocated to the Kuwait Foundation for the Advancement of Sciences <orig>مؤسسة الكويت للتقدم العلمي</orig> account.
        *   Third: A percentage shall be deducted and allocated to the voluntary reserve <orig>الاحتياطي الاختياري</orig> account, as proposed by the Board of Directors <orig>مجلس الإدارة</orig> and approved by the General Assembly <orig>الجمعية العامة</orig>. This deduction shall be stopped by a resolution of the Ordinary General Assembly <orig>الجمعية العامة العادية</orig> based on a proposal from the Board of Directors <orig>مجلس الإدارة</orig>.
        *   Fourth: A portion of the profits shall be deducted based on a proposal from the Board of Directors <orig>مجلس الإدارة</orig> and its report to the General Assembly <orig>الجمعية العامة</orig> to meet the Company's obligations under labor laws <orig>قوانين العمل</orig>. These funds may not be distributed to shareholders.
        *   Fifth: The amount necessary for distributing an initial dividend <orig>حصة أولى من الأرباح</orig> of (5%) five percent to shareholders shall be deducted, as determined by the Board of Directors <orig>مجلس الإدارة</orig> and approved by the General Assembly <orig>الجمعية العامة</orig>.
        *   Sixth: After the foregoing, an amount determined by the Ordinary General Assembly <orig>الجمعية العامة العادية</orig>, not exceeding (10%) ten percent of the remainder, shall be allocated for the Board of Directors' remuneration <orig>مكافآت مجلس الإدارة</orig>.
        *   Seventh: The remaining profits shall then be distributed to shareholders as an additional dividend <orig>حصة إضافية في الأرباح</orig>, or carried forward to the next year based on a proposal from the Board of Directors <orig>مجلس الإدارة</orig>, or allocated to establish a general reserve fund <orig>مال احتياطي عام</orig> or an extraordinary depreciation fund <orig>مال للاستهلاك غير عاديين</orig>.
        *   Eighth: The Ordinary General Assembly <orig>الجمعية العامة العادية</orig> may, based on a proposal from the Board of Directors <orig>مجلس الإدارة</orig>, distribute dividends to shareholders at the end of the financial year <orig>السنة المالية</orig>, or semi-annually. Furthermore, by a resolution of the Ordinary General Assembly <orig>الجمعية العامة العادية</orig> determined annually, the Board of Directors <orig>مجلس الإدارة</orig> may be authorized in advance to distribute dividends semi-annually and to determine the timeline for this distribution. The validity of this distribution is conditional upon it being from actual profits, in accordance with generally accepted accounting principles <orig>المبادئ المحاسبية المتعارف عليها</orig>, and that this distribution does not affect the Company's paid-up capital.
The meeting concluded at 11:15 AM.

Vice Chairman of the Board of Directors <orig>نائب رئيس مجلس الإدارة</orig> and Chief Executive Officer <orig>الرئيس التنفيذي</orig>

They approved the following:
Ratification of the previous agenda minutes, which was approved and ratified.
Item One: Amendment of Article No. 29 in the Articles of Association and Bylaws.
Text of Article 29 of the Bylaws before amendment:
- The Board of Directors <orig>مجلس الإدارة</orig> shall elect by secret ballot a Chairman of the Board <orig>رئيساً للمجلس</orig> and a Vice Chairman <orig>نائباً للرئيس</orig>. The Chairman of the Board of Directors <orig>رئيس مجلس الإدارة</orig> shall represent the company in its relations with third parties and before the judiciary, in addition to the other powers specified in the contract. The signature of the Board of Directors <orig>مجلس الإدارة</orig> shall be considered the company's signature in its relations with third parties, and he shall implement the Board's decisions and adhere to its recommendations. The Vice Chairman <orig>نائب الرئيس</orig> shall act in his absence or if there is an impediment preventing him from exercising his powers.
Text of Article 29 after amendment:
- The Board of Directors <orig>مجلس الإدارة</orig> shall elect by secret ballot a Chairman of the Board <orig>رئيساً للمجلس</orig> and a Vice Chairman <orig>نائباً للرئيس</orig>. The Chairman of the Board of Directors <orig>رئيس مجلس الإدارة</orig> shall have the broadest powers to manage the company and carry out all actions required for the company's management in accordance with its purposes. This authority shall not be limited except by what is stipulated by law, these Bylaws, or the resolutions of the General Assembly <orig>الجمعية العامة</orig>. The Board of Directors <orig>مجلس الإدارة</orig> may borrow, sell, and mortgage the company's real estate, or provide guarantees, arbitration, conciliation, donations, and open and close bank accounts.
The discussion took place, and all attendees approved the aforementioned amendment to the article's text.
In conclusion, the Chairman of the Board of Directors <orig>رئيس مجلس الإدارة</orig> thanked the attendees and concluded the Extraordinary General Assembly <orig>الجمعية العامة غير العادية</orig> meeting at 2:00 PM.
Chairman of the Board of Directors <orig>رئيس مجلس الإدارة</orig>
Kuwait International Takaful Insurance Company <orig>الشركة الكويتية العالمية للتأمين التكافلي</orig>
Minutes of the Extraordinary General Assembly Meeting <orig>محضر اجتماع الجمعية العمومية غير العادية</orig>
Held on 2025/3/23
The Extraordinary General Assembly <orig>الجمعية العمومية غير العادية</orig> of Kuwait International Takaful Insurance Company <orig>الشركة الكويتية العالمية للتأمين التكافلي</orig> met at the company's headquarters located on Arabian Gulf Street <orig>شارع الخليج العربي</orig>, Ahmed Tower <orig>برج أحمد</orig>, at 11:00 AM on Sunday, 2025/03/23, with 100% attendance. The meeting of the General Assembly <orig>الجمعية العمومية</orig> was chaired by the Chairman of the Board of Directors <orig>رئيس مجلس الإدارة</orig> of the company, with the presence of:
1 - Mr. Ghanem Miz'al Fahad Al-Shammari <orig>غانم مزعل فهد الشمري</orig>, Chairman of the Board of Directors <orig>رئيس مجلس الإدارة</orig>
2 - Mr. Abdulaziz Saud Al-Mutairi <orig>عبدالعزيز سعود المطيري</orig>, Vice Chairman of the Board of Directors <orig>نائب رئيس مجلس الإدارة</orig>
3 - Ms. Sahar Majed Faour <orig>سحر ماجد فاعور</orig>, Secretary
4 - Mr. Fahad Abdulrahman Al-Badiwi <orig>فهد عبدالرحمن البديوي</orig>, Gulf Custody Company <orig>الخليجية لحفظ الأوراق المالية</orig>
The General Assembly <orig>الجمعية العمومية</orig> ratified the following items:
1 - Amendment of Article No. (14) of the Bylaws:
Text before amendment:
The company shall be managed by a Board of Directors <orig>مجلس إدارة</orig> composed of (3) three members, from whom the entity or entities authorized to appoint representatives to the Board of Directors <orig>مجلس الإدارة</orig> shall appoint members in proportion to their shareholding in the company, and the General Assembly <orig>الجمعية العمومية العامة</orig> shall elect the remaining members by secret ballot.
Text after amendment:
The company shall be managed by a Board of Directors <orig>مجلس إدارة</orig> composed of (5) five members, from whom the entity or entities authorized to appoint representatives to the Board of Directors <orig>مجلس الإدارة</orig> shall appoint members in proportion to their shareholding in the company, and the General Assembly <orig>الجمعية العمومية العامة</orig> shall elect the remaining members by secret ballot.
2 - Amendment of the text of Article No. (5) of the Articles of Association and Article No. (4) of the Bylaws:
Text before amendment:
The purposes of the company are: The purposes of the company are as stated below, provided that all company transactions are subject to the provisions of the law in accordance with the provisions of Islamic Sharia <orig>الشريعة الإسلامية</orig>, and what does not conflict with the regulating laws and decisions.
1 - Fire insurance.
2 - Accident insurance.
3 - Marine and aviation insurance.
4 - Engineering insurance (equipment, machinery, devices, and electronics).
5 - Motor vehicle insurance (compulsory / supplementary).
6 - Civil liability insurance towards third parties or third-party property.
7 - Health insurance (for two years) covering treatment expenses and surgical operations.
The company shall engage in all cooperative Takaful insurance <orig>التأمين التكافلي التعاوني</orig> activities and what is analogous thereto and related to any activity required for its practice, and carry out insurance and reinsurance operations, conclude all contracts, and undertake all legal actions it deems necessary to achieve its purposes.
To invest all or part of the company's movable or immovable funds in various fields it deems appropriate and in a manner that does not conflict with the regulating laws and decisions related to insurance.
Providing consultations and conducting technical studies in the field of insurance and insurance management for companies or others in the field of Takaful insurance <orig>التأمين التكافلي</orig>.
Owning and acquiring the right to dispose of all movable and immovable funds or any part thereof, or any privileges that the company deems necessary and appropriate for the nature of its work and essential for the growth of its funds.
The company shall directly conduct the aforementioned activities in the State of Kuwait <orig>دولة الكويت</orig> and abroad, either as a principal or by agency. The company may have an interest or participate in any way with entities that engage in similar activities or that may assist it in achieving its purposes in Kuwait <orig>الكويت</orig> or abroad, and it may acquire or merge with such entities.
Text after amendment:
The purposes of the company are as stated below, provided that all company transactions are subject to the provisions of the law in accordance with the provisions of Islamic Sharia <orig>الشريعة الإسلامية</orig>, and what does not conflict with the regulating laws and decisions, and what is required to maintain the objective of achieving cooperation and solidarity among participants.

| 1 | 651107 | Non-Life Takaful Insurance and Fund Formation. |

3 - Amendment of Article No. (25) of the Bylaws:
Text before amendment:
- Without prejudice to the provisions of Companies Law No. 25 of 2012 and its executive regulations
