- 8 Amendment of Article No. (53) of the Articles of Association:
Text Before Amendment:
The provisions of Commercial Companies Law No. 25 of 2012 <orig>قانون الشركات التجارية رقم 25 لسنة 2012</orig>, its amendments, and its executive regulations shall apply to all matters not specifically provided for in the Memorandum of Association or in these Articles.
Text After Amendment:
The provisions of Commercial Companies Law No. 1 of 2016 <orig>قانون الشركات التجارية رقم 1 لسنة 2016</orig>, its amendments, and its executive regulations shall apply to all matters not specifically provided for in the Memorandum of Association or in these Articles.
After reviewing and discussing the items on the agenda, the aforementioned resolutions and amendments were adopted and unanimously approved.
At the conclusion of the meeting, Mr. / Chairman of the Board of Directors and Chief Executive Officer <orig>رئيس مجلس الإدارة والرئيس التنفيذي</orig> thanked the attendees, and the Extraordinary General Assembly meeting concluded at 12:00 PM on the same day.

Chairman of the Board of Directors

Dunya Holding Company (K.S.C.C.) <orig>شركة دنيا القابضة (ش.م.ك.) مقفلة</orig> (Closed)
Minutes of the Extraordinary General Assembly Meeting
The Extraordinary General Assembly of the shareholders of Dunya Holding Company <orig>شركة دنيا القابضة</orig> - a Kuwaiti Shareholding Company (Holding) <orig>شركة مساهمة كويتية (قابضة)</orig> - held its extraordinary meeting to add a new article to the company's Articles of Association, at 10:45 AM on Monday, March 24, 2025, at the company's headquarters located in Shuwaikh Industrial Area Three <orig>الشويخ الصناعية الثالثة</orig> - Block A - Plot 98 - Mezzanine.
The meeting was chaired by Mr. Ali Abdul Hamid Al-Qattan <orig>علي عبد الحميد القطان</orig> - Vice Chairman of the Board of Directors and Chief Executive Officer.
Also present at the meeting were:
- Mr. Fahad Abdul Rahman Al-Badiwi <orig>فهد عبد الرحمن البديوي</orig> - representing Gulf Custody Company <orig>الشركة الخليجية لحفظ الأوراق المالية</orig> - in my capacity as Board Secretary.
- Shareholders holding 21,000,000 shares, in person and by proxy, representing 100% of the total paid-up share capital of the company, amounting to 21,000,000 shares.
After the announcement of the quorum for the Extraordinary General Assembly meeting, the Chairman of the session opened the meeting, welcoming the attendees, and then proceeded to present the items on the agenda of the Extraordinary General Assembly. Accordingly, after reviewing the agenda, the following resolution was adopted:
* Approval was given to add a new article to the company's Articles of Association, to be numbered (76), with the following text:
The shareholder's right to dispose of their shares shall be restricted by the following two limitations:
1- Requiring a right of first refusal for the company's shareholders to purchase shares that their owner wishes to sell.
2- Requiring the Board of Directors' approval for the share purchaser.
Dispositions referred to in Companies Law No. 1 of 2016 <orig>قانون الشركات رقم 1 لسنة 2016</orig> are exempted from these two limitations.
- Without prejudice to the provisions of Companies Law No. 1 of 2016 <orig>قانون الشركات رقم 1 لسنة 2016</orig> and its executive regulations, the Ordinary General Assembly shall determine the remuneration of the Board of Directors' members.
- 4 Amendment of Article No. (29) of the Articles of Association, Clause No. 4:
Text Before Amendment:
- Any modern communication means specified in the executive regulations of Companies Law No. 25 of 2012 <orig>قانون الشركات رقم 25 لسنة 2012</orig> and its amendments. The Ministry of Commerce and Industry <orig>وزارة التجارة والصناعة</orig> must be notified in writing of the agenda, date, and place of the meeting, generally at least, for its representative to attend.
Text After Amendment:
- Any modern communication means specified in the executive regulations of Companies Law No. 1 of 2016 <orig>قانون الشركات رقم 1 لسنة 2016</orig> and its amendments. The Ministry of Commerce and Industry <orig>وزارة التجارة والصناعة</orig> must be notified in writing of the agenda, date, and place of the meeting, generally at least, for its representative to attend.
- 5 Amendment of Article No. (36) of the Articles of Association:
Text Before Amendment:
The Annual General Assembly shall convene upon an invitation from the Board of Directors within three months following the end of the fiscal year, at the time and place designated by the Board of Directors. The Board may invite the General Assembly to meet whenever necessary. The Board of Directors must issue an invitation for the General Assembly to meet upon a reasoned request from a number of shareholders owning ten percent of the company's capital, or upon a request from the auditor, within fifteen days from the date of the request. The agenda shall be prepared by the inviting party.
The provisions related to the founding assembly stipulated in Companies Law No. 25 of 2012 <orig>قانون الشركات رقم 25 لسنة 2012</orig> and its amendments shall apply to the procedures for inviting the General Assembly, the quorum for attendance, and voting.
Text After Amendment:
The Annual General Assembly shall convene upon an invitation from the Board of Directors within three months following the end of the fiscal year, at the time and place designated by the Board of Directors. The Board may invite the General Assembly to meet whenever necessary. The Board of Directors must issue an invitation for the General Assembly to meet upon a reasoned request from a number of shareholders owning ten percent of the company's capital, or upon a request from the auditor, within fifteen days from the date of the request. The agenda shall be prepared by the inviting party.
The provisions related to the founding assembly stipulated in Companies Law No. 1 of 2016 <orig>قانون الشركات رقم 1 لسنة 2016</orig> and its amendments shall apply to the procedures for inviting the General Assembly, the quorum for attendance, and voting.
- 6 Amendment of Article No. (51) of the Articles of Association:
Text Before Amendment:
The company shall be dissolved for one of the reasons stipulated in Companies Law No. 25 of 2012 <orig>قانون الشركات رقم 25 لسنة 2012</orig>, its amendments, and its executive regulations.
Text After Amendment:
The company shall be dissolved for one of the reasons stipulated in Companies Law No. 1 of 2016 <orig>قانون الشركات رقم 1 لسنة 2016</orig>, its amendments, and its executive regulations.
- 7 Amendment of Article No. (52) of the Articles of Association:

8- If, upon studying the tender, the Ministry finds any error or omission, or if the technical documents or bills of quantities reveal anything that affects the categories of its bid or the value of the works, the tenderer must seek clarification from the Ministry of Education <orig>وزارة التربية</orig> before submitting its bid. The Ministry will study these observations and inquiries, respond to them, and rectify any error, omission, ambiguity, or contradiction (if any). This shall not entail any additional responsibility or obligation on the Ministry.
9- Tender documents shall be deposited in the bids box at the Supplies and Warehouses Department in South Subhan <orig>صبحان الجنوبي</orig> area during official working hours, no later than (10) ten days from the date of announcement publication, at 12:00 PM sharp, according to the decision issued by the Ministry regarding changing or extending the closing date. No bid received after the stipulated closing date will be accepted, nor will any amendment to the prices of submitted bids received after bid submission be considered.
10- The tenderer must fill in the attached tables and submit a statement of all necessary supplies for executing the works subject of the tender – if any – within the same bid documents submitted. The Ministry reserves the right to reject the bid unless it includes the filled tables in accordance with public interest, with the necessity of adhering to what is stated in the technical specifications and conditions of the tender.
11- The tenderer must submit all bank guarantees related to this tender in Arabic.
12- A preliminary meeting will be held five days after the announcement.

3- The shareholder must notify the company of the terms of sale before disposing of their shares. The disposal of shares shall not be effective until ten days have elapsed from the date of notification without any shareholder submitting a request to purchase the shares. If a shareholder comes forward to purchase the shares, it must be at the price stated in the terms of sale.
4- Without prejudice to the provisions regarding the company's purchase of its own shares, the Board of Directors, in case of rejecting the buyer's person, must purchase the shares for the company's account within ten days from the date of notifying the Board of Directors of the approval request. In this case, the purchase shall be at the price agreed upon by the shareholder for selling their shares.
(All of the above is subject to the approval of the competent regulatory authorities)
Before the end of the meeting, the Chairman of the session, Mr. Ali Abdul Hamid Al-Qattan <orig>علي عبد الحميد القطان</orig>, thanked the attendees and concluded the ordinary general assembly meeting at 11:00 AM on the same day.

Ministry of Interior <orig>وزارة الداخلية</orig>
Notice
Regarding the Extension of the Tender Closing Date
No. (L.Sh 2024/205. 2025)
Supply, Installation, Operation, and Maintenance of a Wastewater Treatment Unit on Qaruh <orig>قاروه</orig> and Umm Al-Maradim <orig>أم المرادم</orig> Islands for the General Directorate of Construction and Maintenance – Ministry of Interior <orig>وزارة الداخلية</orig>
Please be informed that the closing date (bid submission) for the aforementioned tender has been extended to Wednesday, 7/5/2025, at the Bid Opening Committee in the Ministry of Interior <orig>وزارة الداخلية</orig> building (East Area – Al-Siddiq School – First Floor) from 8:00 AM until 1:00 PM. Notice
Regarding the Amendment of the Tender Closing Day
No. (2024/5. 2025) Repair, Maintenance, Replacement, and Operation Works for Fuel Steps and their Accessories for the General Directorate of Coastal Drilling for the General Directorate of Construction and Maintenance – Ministry of Interior <orig>وزارة الداخلية</orig>
Please be informed that the closing day (bid submission) for the aforementioned tender has been amended to Wednesday, 7/5/2025, at the Bid Opening Committee in the Ministry of Interior <orig>وزارة الداخلية</orig> building (East Area – Al-Siddiq School – First Floor) from 8:00 AM until 1:00 PM. Ministry of Education <orig>وزارة التربية</orig>
Re-issuance of Tender No. M.M / 2024/31-2025
The Ministry of Education <orig>وزارة التربية</orig> announces the issuance of a (public) tender for leasing 20 half-lorries with drivers and handling workers, in accordance with the technical conditions and specifications in the tender documents.
General Guidelines for the Tender:
1- The tender is (public) for approved tenderers with the Ministry of Education <orig>وزارة التربية</orig>.
2- It is a condition for those applying for this tender that they must be specialized institutions/companies within Kuwait in the works subject of the tender, registered in the Commercial Register and the Kuwait Chamber of Commerce and Industry <orig>غرفة تجارة و صناعة الكويت</orig> for the current year, and a certificate to that effect, dated concurrently with the tender issuance date, must be attached to their bid.
3- This tender is (non-divisible), and the bidder is not entitled to submit alternative offers.
4- The financial cost for obtaining a copy of the tender documents is (75) seventy-five Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig> only.
5- The bid must be accompanied by an initial security deposit of no less than (K.D. 2000) two thousand Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig> only. This security must be in the form of a certified check or a letter of guarantee from a bank accredited in the State of Kuwait <orig>دولة الكويت</orig>, issued in the name of the bidder and in favor of the Ministry of Education <orig>وزارة التربية</orig>, and not subject to any restriction or condition. Bids not accompanied by this security, or accompanied by security that violates any of the mentioned regulations, will not be considered. The security must be valid for the required bid validity period.
6- The total duration of the contract is three months from the date of signing the contract, during which the contractor is committed to executing the tender works in accordance with the general and special conditions, provisions, and technical specifications in the tender documents.

Ministry of Health <orig>وزارة الصحة</orig>
Announcement
The Ministry of Health <orig>وزارة الصحة</orig> (Medical Warehouses Department <orig>إدارة المستودعات الطبية</orig> - Medical Supplies Control <orig>مراقبة اللوازم الطبية</orig>) announces the offering of the following practices:

<table_caption>Medical Supplies Tenders from Ministry of Health</table_caption>
<table>
| Practice No. | Description                                                                                                                            | Fees | Closing Date                   |
|:-------------|:---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------|:-----|:-------------------------------|
| 5ANF02       | Medical consumables for Anesthesia and Intensive Care Unit rooms, for Al-Farwaniyah Hospital <orig>مستشفى الفروانية</orig>             | 75   | 30 days from announcement date or more |
| 5CS003       | Non-sterile cotton chairs for sterilization departments in all hospitals                                                               | 75   | 30 days from announcement date or more |
| 5CS004       | Gauze pads for abdomen, size 20cm*50cm, X-ray detectable, for sterilization departments in all hospitals                               | 75   | 30 days from announcement date or more |
| 5CS005       | Paper sterilization bags, size 140mm * 50mm * 330mm, for sterilization departments in all hospitals                                   | 75   | 30 days from announcement date or more |
| 5CS007       | Paper sterilization bags, size 90mm*50mm*150mm, for sterilization departments in all hospitals                                        | 75   | 30 days from announcement date or more |

| 5DB012       | Needle size 21, for all departments in health centers and hospitals                                                                   | 75   | 30 days from announcement date or more |
| 5MEK01       | PICC LINE consumables, for Kuwait Cancer Control Center <orig>مركز الكويت لمكافحة السرطان</orig>                                       | 75   | 30 days from announcement date or more |
| 5TX001       | Post-partum female diapers, for all departments in health centers and hospitals                                                        | 75   | 30 days from announcement date or more |
</table>

Bids shall be placed in the bid box at the Medical Warehouses Department <orig>إدارة المستودعات الطبية</orig>, and bids must be valid for a period of (90 days) from the closing date.
Companies wishing to participate in the practice must meet the following conditions:
1- Local companies must be registered with the Medical Warehouses Department <orig>إدارة المستودعات الطبية</orig> in the suppliers' register.
2- Local companies must specialize in the medical field and be certified by an accredited certificate from the Chamber of Commerce and Industry <orig>غرفة التجارة والصناعة</orig>.
3- When submitting two offers, two booklets must be purchased with different receipts.
4- Attach a valid product registration certificate from the Department of Drug and Herbal Medicine Registration and Control <orig>إدارة التسجيل ومراقبة الأدوية الطبية والنباتية</orig>, or proof of submission of the certificate, and a copy of the manufacturer's and material's registration in the suppliers' register at the Medical Warehouses Department <orig>إدارة المستودعات الطبية</orig> within the contents of the submitted bid (specific to Drug Control <orig>مراقبة الأدوية</orig>).
5- Provide samples of new materials, whether a new product requested for the first time or from a new manufacturer, for the specialized control (Drugs <orig>الأدوية</orig> – Medical Supplies <orig>اللوازم الطبية</orig>).
6- Attach a certificate of national labor support percentage.
7- Practice documents can be obtained from the Ministry of Health's <orig>وزارة الصحة</orig> official website.
8- The fee for purchasing the booklet can be paid through the website to be attached with the practice documents.
9- Submit price offers in a sealed envelope, including practice documents, according to the closing date specified on the Ministry of Health's <orig>وزارة الصحة</orig> official website.

The following conditions apply to companies wishing to participate in the tender:
1- The local company must be registered with the Medical Warehouses Department <orig>إدارة المستودعات الطبية</orig> in the Suppliers Register.
2- The local company must specialize in the medical field and be certified with an accredited certificate from the Chamber of Commerce and Industry <orig>غرفة التجارة والصناعة</orig>.

Announcement
The Ministry of Health <orig>وزارة الصحة</orig> (Medical Warehouses Department <orig>إدارة المستودعات الطبية</orig> - Medical Supplies Control <orig>مراقبة اللوازم الطبية</orig>) announces the offering of the following tenders:

| No. | Tender No. | Description | Fees | Closing Date |
|:----|:---|:------|:-------|:---|
| 1   | 5CD101      | Cardiac consumables, specifically for the Cardiac Catheterization Unit, for the needs of Al-Sadri Hospital <orig>مستشفى الصدري</orig> | 150    | 30 days from the announcement date or more |
| 2   | 4DB077      | Electrodes for cardiac resuscitation devices, for the needs of all departments in health centers and hospitals | 300    | 30 days from the announcement date or more |
| 3   | 4DXM27      | Consumables for radiology and radiotherapy, for the needs of Mubarak Hospital <orig>مستشفى مبارك</orig> | 75     | 20 days from the announcement date or more |
</table>

Bids must be placed in the bids box at the Medical Warehouses Department <orig>إدارة المستودعات الطبية</orig>, and bids must be valid for a period of (90 days) from the closing date.
The following conditions apply to companies wishing to participate in the tender:
1- The local company must be registered with the Medical Warehouses Department <orig>إدارة المستودعات الطبية</orig> in the Suppliers Register.
2- The local company must specialize in the medical field and be certified with an accredited certificate from the Chamber of Commerce and Industry <orig>غرفة التجارة والصناعة</orig>.
3- When submitting two offers, two booklets and two different receipts must be purchased.
4- Attach a valid product registration certificate from the Department of Registration and Control of Medical and Herbal Medicines <orig>إدارة التسجيل ومراقبة الأدوية الطبية والنباتية</orig>, or proof of submission of the certificate, and a copy of the manufacturer's and material's registration in the Suppliers Register at the Medical Warehouses Department <orig>إدارة المستودعات الطبية</orig> within the contents of the submitted bid (specifically for Medicines Control <orig>مراقبة الأدوية</orig>).
5- Provide samples of new materials, whether a new product requested for the first time or from a new manufacturer, for the competent authority (Medicines – Medical Supplies <orig>اللوازم الطبية</orig>).
6- Attach a certificate of national labor support percentage.
7- Tender documents can be obtained from the Ministry of Health's <orig>وزارة الصحة</orig> official website.
8- The fee for purchasing the booklet can be paid through the website to be attached with the tender documents.
9- Submit price offers in a sealed envelope, including the tender documents, according to the closing date specified on the Ministry of Health's <orig>وزارة الصحة</orig> official website.

Companies wishing to participate in the practice must meet the following conditions:

Announcement

The following conditions apply to companies wishing to participate in the practice:
1- The local company must be registered with the Medical Warehouses Department in the suppliers' register.
2- The local company must specialize in the medical field and be certified by an accredited certificate from the Chamber of Commerce and Industry.
3- Submission of two offers with purchase prices for two different tender documents.
4- Attaching a valid product registration certificate from the Department of Registration and Control of Medical Drugs, or proof of submission of the certificate, and a copy of the manufacturer's and material's registration in the suppliers' register at the Medical Warehouses Department, as part of the tender contents submitted in the (Drug Control Brochure/Tender Document).
5- Submission of samples for new materials, whether a new product requested for the first time or from a new manufacturer, for specialized control (medicines - medical supplies).
6- Attaching a certificate of national labor support percentage.
7- Practice documents can be obtained from the Ministry of Health's <orig>وزارة الصحة</orig> official website.
8- The practice brochure/tender document fees must be paid through the website and attached with the practice documents.
9- Submission of price offers in a sealed envelope, inclusive with the practice documents, according to the closing date specified on the Ministry of Health's <orig>وزارة الصحة</orig> official website.

Minutes of the Meeting of the Births and Deaths Committee <orig>لجنة المواليد والوفيات</orig> at its session
No. 9/2025, held on 16/3/2025
Formed by Ministerial Decision No. 1650/2021
The Births and Deaths Committee <orig>لجنة المواليد والوفيات</orig>, stipulated in Article 15 of Law No. 36/93 and formed by Ministerial Decision No. 1650/2021, met.
Mr. / Director of the Central Register Department for Births and Deaths <orig>إدارة السجل المركزي للمواليد والوفيات</orig> | Chairman
Mr. / Head of the General Medical Council <orig>المجلس الطبي العام</orig> | Member
Mr. / Head of the Research and Opinion Department <orig>قسم البحوث والرأي</orig> | Member
Mr. / Head of the Registration Department <orig>قسم القيد</orig> | Member
Mr. / Head of the Deaths Department <orig>قسم الوفيات</orig> | Member
Mr. / Legal Researcher <orig>الباحث القانوني</orig> | Member
Mr. / Head of the Records Department <orig>قسم السجلات</orig> | Member
Ms. Alia Al-Saffar <orig>علياء الصفار</orig> acted as the Committee Secretary.
The Committee reviewed applications from No. ((115)) to No. ((127)) in the attached list, pertaining to data amendments in birth and death registers for dropped birth and death registration applications.
The Committee, after its review and ensuring the completeness of documents and records, decided to announce the amendments and applications in the Official Gazette (Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig>) in two consecutive issues. This is so that if the legal period (fifteen days) from the date of the last announcement expires and no objection is submitted, the amendments will be made in the registers and birth and death certificates will be issued.
Head of the Research and Opinion Department <orig>قسم البحوث والرأي</orig> | Head of the Registration Department <orig>قسم القيد</orig> | Head of the Deaths Department <orig>قسم الوفيات</orig> | Head of the Records Department <orig>قسم السجلات</orig>
Legal Researcher <orig>الباحث القانوني</orig> | Committee Secretary | Head of the General Medical Council <orig>المجلس الطبي العام</orig> | Director of the Central Register Department for Births <orig>إدارة السجل المركزي للمواليد</orig>
<page_end>56</page_end>

The court ordered his deportation from the country immediately upon the execution of the pronounced sentence.

**In Case No.:** 003291 / 20 – Commercial Affairs Prosecution <orig>نيابة شئون تجاري</orig> - Commercial Misdemeanors <orig>جنح تجارية</orig>

**Original Case No.:** 200964570

**Nationality:** Philippines <orig>الفلبين</orig> **Civil ID No.:** 263121502941
**An absentia judgment ruling:** to fine the accused 500 KWD <orig>دك</orig> for what was attributed to him.
And the Public Prosecution <orig>النيابة العامة</orig> announces the judgment against him with this ruling and instructs all security authorities <orig>جهات الامن</orig> to enforce it
in accordance with the text of Article 188 of the Code of Criminal Procedures and Trials <orig>قانون الاجراءات والمحاكمات الجزائية</orig>, noting that if

an absentia judgment ruling: to fine the accused female ten dinars for each value

<page_metadata>
{
  "page_title": "Official Auction Announcements <orig>إعلانات المزاد العلني</orig>",
  "document_date": "2025-04-06",
  "issue_number": 1733,
  "volume_number": 71,
  "document_type": "official_gazette",
  "languages_detected": ["ar"],
  "page_type": "content",
  "authors": null,
  "publisher": "Kuwait Today / Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig>",
  "page_summary": "This page contains two official announcements from the Kuwaiti Courts regarding public auctions for real estate properties, detailing the properties, auction dates, basic prices, and conditions for participation and payment, along with legal references."
}
</page_metadata>
<header>
63
Kuwait Today / Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig> Issue 1733, Seventy-First Year
Sunday, 8 Shawwal 1446 AH - 6/4/2025 CE
</header>
The defaulting bidder shall be liable for any deficit in the property's price.
Sixth: In all cases, the successful bidder shall bear the property transfer and registration fees, execution procedure expenses amounting to 200 K.D. <orig>د.ك</orig>, legal and expert fees, and advertising and publication costs for the sale in daily newspapers.
Seventh: This announcement is published in application of the law and at the request of those directly involved in the sale procedures and under their responsibility, without the Clerk's Office <orig>إدارة الكتاب</orig> at the General Court <orig>المحكمة الكلية</orig> bearing any responsibility.
Eighth: The successful bidder acknowledges that they have inspected the property in a manner that negates any ignorance.
Notice: 1- This sale announcement shall be published in the Official Gazette <orig>الجريدة الرسمية</orig> in accordance with Article 266 of the Code of Civil Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig>.
2- The auction award judgment is subject to appeal within seven days from the date of its pronouncement, in accordance with Article 277 of the Code of Civil Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig>.
3- The last paragraph of Article 276 of the Code of Civil Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig> states that "If the dispossessed owner is residing in the property, they shall remain therein as a tenant by operation of law, and the successful bidder shall be obligated to draw up a lease contract in their favor at the fair market rent."
President of the General Court <orig>المحكمة الكلية</orig>

## Announcement of Property Sale by Public Auction
The Clerk's Office <orig>إدارة الكتاب</orig> at the General Court <orig>المحكمة الكلية</orig> announces the public auction of the property described below, on Thursday, 1/5/2025 CE, in Hall 52, on the second floor of the Palace of Justice <orig>قصر العدل</orig>, at 9:00 AM, in execution of the court judgment issued in lawsuit No. 2024/39 Sales/3.

### Filed by:
First: Mariam Ahmed Ali Al-Kandari <orig>مريم أحمد علي الكندري</orig>.
Second: Sadiqah Ahmed Ali Al-Kandari <orig>صديقة أحمد علي الكندري</orig>.

### Against:
1- Mariam Farad Khadnak <orig>مريم فرض خدنك</orig>.
2- Hessa Ahmed Ali Hassan Al-Kandari <orig>حصة أحمد علي حسن الكندري</orig>.
3- Haneen Ahmed Ali Hassan Al-Kandari <orig>حنين أحمد علي حسن الكندري</orig>.
4- Abeer Ahmed Ali Hassan Al-Kandari <orig>عبير أحمد علي حسن الكندري</orig>.
5- Shareefah Ahmed Ali Hassan Al-Kandari <orig>شريفه أحمد علي حسن الكندري</orig>.
6- Sarah Ahmed Ali Hassan Al-Kandari <orig>ساره أحمد علي حسن الكندري</orig>.
7- Suad Ahmed Ali Hassan Al-Kandari <orig>سعاد أحمد علي حسن الكندري</orig>.
8- Heirs of the late / Ali Ahmed Ali Hassan Al-Kandari <orig>علي أحمد علي حسن الكندري</orig>.
a- Kulthum Ahmed Mohammed Talib <orig>كلثوم أحمد محمد طالب</orig>.

Property Description (According to the attached Certificate of Description)
Property Document No. 5826/2016, located in Al-Na'eem <orig>النعيم</orig> area - Plot (227), Block No. (1), Plan M/37704 - with an area of 400m², by public auction with a base price of 420,000 K.D. <orig>د.ك</orig> (Four Hundred Twenty Thousand Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig>).

** According to the Certificate of Description:
Private residence consisting of a ground floor, first floor, and a partial second floor. There is an unlicensed elevator, and violation report No. 5431 was issued on 1/2/2024 CE. The violation is still ongoing, and this is for your information.

** According to the Certificate of Description:
The disputed property located in Al-Na'eem <orig>النعيم</orig> area - Block 1 - Street 18 - Plot 227 - House 3 at the time of inspection is as follows:
- The disputed property is a residential plot located on a single cul-de-sac street, bordered by neighbors on 3 sides, and consists of two and a half floors with a white mosaic facade.
- The property's area is 400m² according to the document.
- The disputed property's air conditioning is central, with some units being conventional.
- Ordinary interior finishes.
- Bathroom and washbasins - room with bathroom - preparatory kitchen - main kitchen.
- Ground Floor: Reception hall with bathroom and washbasins - living room - diwaniya <orig>ديوانية</orig> with bathroom and washbasins - driver's room - room with bathroom - preparatory kitchen - main kitchen.
- First Floor: Master bedroom with bathroom and dressing room - 4 rooms with two bathrooms - preparatory kitchen - living room open to the corridor.
- Half Floor with Roof: Room - bathroom - preparatory kitchen - hall.

Second: Auction Conditions:
First: The auction shall commence at the base price. Participation in the auction requires payment of at least one-fifth of that price by a certified check from the drawee bank or by a letter of guarantee from one of the banks in favor of the Execution Department <orig>إدارة التنفيذ</orig> at the Ministry of Justice <orig>وزارة العدل</orig>.
Second: The bidder whose offer is approved by the judge must deposit the full approved price, expenses, and registration fees at the time of the sale session.
Third: If the bidder whose offer was approved does not deposit the full price, they must deposit at least one-fifth of the price; otherwise, the bidding shall be re-opened at their expense in the same session based on the price at which the sale was previously awarded.
Fourth: If the bidder deposits in the subsequent session, the auction award judgment shall be against them, unless someone comes forward in that session who accepts to purchase with a ten percent increase, accompanied by the deposit of the full auction price. In this case, the bidding shall be re-opened in the same session based on this price.
This is the announcement for bidding in the same session based on this price.

<page_metadata>
{
  "page_title": "Kuwait Today Official Gazette - Legal Announcements and Property Auction",
  "document_date": "2025-04-06",
  "issue_number": 1733,
  "volume_number": 71,
  "document_type": "official_gazette",
  "languages_detected": ["ar"],
  "page_type": "content",
  "authors": null,
  "publisher": "Kuwait Today / Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig>",
  "page_summary": "This page of the official gazette contains legal announcements, including a detailed notice for a public auction of a property, outlining the sale procedures and listing the parties involved in the associated legal cases."
}
</page_metadata>
<header>
67
Sunday, 8 Shawwal 1446 AH - 6/4/2025 CE
Kuwait Today / Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig> No. 1733, Seventy-First Year
</header>

Secondly: The person whose bid is approved by the judge must deposit the full approved price, expenses, and registration fees immediately upon the sale session being held.
Thirdly: If the person whose bid is approved does not deposit the full price, they must deposit at least one-fifth of the price; otherwise, the bidding will be reopened at their expense in the same session based on the price at which the sale was previously awarded.
Fourthly: If the bidder deposits the price in the subsequent session, the auction will be awarded to them, unless someone comes forward in that session willing to purchase with a ten percent increase, accompanied by the deposit of the full auction price. In this case, the bidding will be reopened in the same session based on this new price.
Fifthly: If the initial bidder fails to deposit the full price in the subsequent session, and no one comes forward to bid with a ten percent increase, the bidding will immediately be reopened at their expense based on the price at which it was previously awarded to them in the preceding session. In this session, no bid not accompanied by a full deposit of its value will be considered. The defaulting bidder shall be liable for any shortfall in the property's price.
Sixthly: In all cases, the successful bidder shall bear the transfer and property registration fees, execution procedure expenses amounting to 200 Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>د.ك</orig>, legal and expert fees, and advertising and publication costs for the sale in daily newspapers.
Seventhly: This announcement shall be published in accordance with the law, and those directly responsible for the sale procedures shall do so at their own responsibility, without the Department of Clerks <orig>إدارة الكتاب</orig> at the General Court <orig>المحكمة الكلية</orig> bearing any liability.
Eighthly: The successful bidder acknowledges that they have inspected the property in a manner that negates any ignorance of its condition.
Notice: 1- This sale announcement shall be published in the Official Gazette <orig>الجريدة الرسمية</orig> in accordance with Article 266 of the Code of Civil Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig>.
2- The auction award judgment is subject to appeal within seven days from the date of its pronouncement, in accordance with Article 277 of the Code of Civil Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig>.
3- The last paragraph of Article 276 of the Code of Civil Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig> states that "If the person whose ownership has been divested is residing in the property, they shall remain therein as a tenant by operation of law, and the successful bidder shall be obligated to draw up a lease contract in their favor at a fair market rent."
President of the General Court <orig>المحكمة الكلية</orig>

  "authors": null,
  "publisher": "Kuwait Today / Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig>",
  "page_summary": "This page details the conditions and procedures for a property sale by public auction, including payment terms, legal requirements, and a list of involved parties and property descriptions."
}
</page_metadata>
<header>
68
Kuwait Today / Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig> Issue 1733, Seventy-First Year
Sunday, 8 Shawwal 1446 AH - 6/4/2025 AD
</header>
the sale had been awarded to him.
Fourth: If the bidder deposits the price in the subsequent session, the auction shall be awarded to him, unless someone comes forward in that session who accepts to purchase with a ten percent increase, accompanied by the deposit of the full auction price. In this case, the bidding shall be re-opened in the same session based on this price.
Fifth: If the first bidder fails to deposit the full price in the subsequent session, and no one comes forward to bid with a ten percent increase immediately on his account based on the price at which it was awarded to him in the previous session, no bid in this session shall be considered unless accompanied by a deposit of its full value. The defaulting bidder shall be liable for any shortfall in the property's price.
Sixth: In all cases, the successful bidder shall bear the transfer and registration fees for ownership, the advertising and execution expenses amounting to 200 Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>د.ك</orig>, legal and expert fees, and the costs of advertising and publishing the sale in daily newspapers.
Seventh: This announcement is published in accordance with the law, and bidders are requested for the sale procedures at their own responsibility, without the Clerk's Office <orig>إدارة الكتاب</orig> at the General Court <orig>المحكمة الكلية</orig> bearing any liability.
Eighth: The successful bidder acknowledges that he has inspected the property with an inspection that negates any ignorance.
Notice:
1- This sale announcement shall be published in the Official Gazette <orig>الجريدة الرسمية</orig> in accordance with Article 266 of the Code of Civil Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig>.
2- The auction award judgment is subject to appeal within seven days from the date of its pronouncement, in accordance with Article 277 of the Code of Civil Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig>.
3- The last paragraph of Article 276 of the Code of Civil Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig> states that "If the dispossessed owner is residing in the property, he shall remain therein as a tenant by force of law, and the successful bidder shall be obliged to draw up a lease contract in his favor at a fair market rent."

President of the General Court <orig>المحكمة الكلية</orig>

Heirs of the late / Bana Abdullah Fahad Al-Azmi <orig>بنه عبدالله فهد العازمي</orig>, namely:

Plot M/36874 <orig>م/36874</orig> with an area of 301m2, by public auction, with a base price of K.D. 300,000 (Three Hundred Thousand Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig>).
** According to the description certificate <orig>شهادة الأوصاف</orig>:
- No violations found.
** According to the expert's report <orig>تقرير الخبير</orig>:
The property subject to the dispute, located in Al-Firdous <orig>الفردوس</orig> area – Block 2 – Street 1 – Avenue – House 3, automated address number 12821201, at the time of inspection, is as follows:
1. The property subject to the dispute conforms in terms of general and specific specifications and boundaries to document number 1993/4297, with an area of 301m2.
2. The property subject to the dispute is a private residence house overlooking two streets (corner), Street No. (1) and Avenue No. (8).
3. The property subject to the dispute consists of a ground floor and a first floor, with the following details:
    *   a- The ground floor consists of 2 rooms + bathroom + hall + kitchen + external diwaniya <orig>ديوانية</orig> with bathroom.
    *   b- The first floor consists of 5 rooms + 3 bathrooms + hall.
4. The exterior cladding is limestone.
5. The house air conditioning consists of split units.

Secondly: Auction Conditions:
*   Firstly: The auction begins at the base price, and participation in the auction requires payment of at least one-fifth of that price by a certified check from the drawee bank or by a letter of guarantee from one of the banks in favor of the Enforcement Department <orig>إدارة التنفيذ</orig> at the Ministry of Justice <orig>وزارة العدل</orig>.
*   Secondly: The bidder whose offer is approved by the judge must deposit the full approved price, expenses, and registration fees at the time of the sale session.
*   Thirdly: If the bidder whose offer was approved does not deposit the full price, they must deposit at least one-fifth of the price, otherwise the bidding will be reopened at their expense in the same session based on the price at which the sale was initially awarded.
*   Fourthly: If the bidder deposits the price in the subsequent session, the auction will be awarded to them, unless someone comes forward in that session willing to purchase with a ten percent increase, accompanied by the deposit of the full auction price. In this case, the bidding will be reopened in the same session based on this new price.
*   Fifthly: If the first bidder does not deposit the full price in the subsequent session and no one comes forward with a ten percent increase, the bidding will immediately be reopened at their expense based on the price at which it was awarded to them in the previous session. In this session, no offer not accompanied by a full deposit of its value will be considered. The defaulting bidder shall be liable for any decrease in the property's price.
*   Sixthly: In all cases, the successful bidder shall bear the transfer and registration fees for ownership, enforcement procedure expenses amounting to K.D. 200, legal and expert fees, and advertising and publication costs for the sale in daily newspapers.
*   Seventhly: This announcement is published in application of the law and is requested by those directly involved in the sale procedures, at their responsibility, without the Clerk's Office <orig>إدارة الكتاب</orig> at the General Court <orig>المحكمة الكلية</orig> bearing any responsibility.
*   Eighthly: The successful bidder acknowledges that they have inspected the property in a manner that negates any ignorance.

Notice:
1. This sale announcement shall be published in the Official Gazette <orig>الجريدة الرسمية</orig> in accordance with Article 266 of the Code of Civil Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig>.
2. The auction award judgment is subject to appeal within seven days from the date of its pronouncement, in accordance with Article 277 of the Code of Civil Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig>.
3. The last paragraph of Article 276 of the Code of Civil Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig> states that "If the dispossessed owner is residing in the property, they shall remain in it as a tenant by operation of law, and the successful bidder shall be obligated to draw up a lease contract in their favor at a fair market rent."

Kuwait Today / Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig> Issue 1733, Seventy-First Year

60m2.
- The property consists of a ground floor, first floor, roof, and two annexes. The first annex consists of a diwaniya <orig>ديوانية</orig>, bathroom, washbasins, storage room, and a room. Above the first annex is an apartment consisting of a living room, two bedrooms, a bathroom, and a kitchen. The second annex consists of a kitchen. The second annex consists of two floors, each floor having an apartment consisting of two bedrooms, a bathroom, and a kitchen.
The ground floor of the property consists of two living rooms and a kitchen with two entrances, one from inside the property and the other from outside. The first floor consists of two apartments; the first apartment consists of a living room, two bedrooms, a bathroom, and a kitchen, while the second apartment consists of two bedrooms and a bathroom.
Secondly: Auction Terms and Conditions:
First: The auction shall commence at the basic price. Participation in the auction requires payment of at least one-fifth of that price by a certified check from the drawee bank or by a letter of guarantee from one of the banks in favor of the Enforcement Department <orig>إدارة التنفيذ</orig> at the Ministry of Justice <orig>وزارة العدل</orig>.
Second: Whoever's bid is approved by the judge must deposit the full approved price, expenses, and registration fees at the time of the sale session.
Third: If the bidder whose bid was approved does not deposit the full price, they must deposit at least one-fifth of the price; otherwise, the bidding will be re-opened at their expense in the same session based on the price at which the sale was previously awarded.
Fourth: If the bidder deposits the price in the subsequent session, the auction award judgment will be issued in their favor, unless someone comes forward in that session who accepts to purchase with a ten percent increase, calculated by depositing the full price. In this case, the bidding will be re-opened in the same session based on this new price.
Fifth: If the first bidder fails to deposit the full price in the subsequent session and no one comes forward to bid with the ten percent increase, the bidding will immediately be re-opened at their expense based on the price at which it was awarded to them in the previous session. In this session, no bid not accompanied by a full deposit of its value will be considered. The defaulting bidder shall be liable for any shortfall in the property's price.
Sixth: In all cases, the successful bidder shall bear the transfer and registration fees for ownership, enforcement procedure expenses amounting to 200 K.D. <orig>د.ك</orig>, legal and expert fees, and advertising and publication costs for the sale in daily newspapers.
Seventh: This announcement is published in application of the law, and those directly involved in the sale procedures are responsible for them, without the Clerk's Office <orig>إدارة الكتاب</orig> at the General Court <orig>المحكمة الكلية</orig> bearing any responsibility.
Eighth: The successful bidder acknowledges that they have inspected the property with an inspection that negates any ignorance.
Notice: 1- The auction award judgment is subject to appeal within seven days from the date of its pronouncement, in accordance with Article 277 of the Code of Civil Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig>.
2- The last paragraph of Article 276 of the Code of Civil Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig> states that "If the dispossessed owner is residing in the property, they shall remain in it as a tenant by operation of law, and the successful bidder shall be obligated to draw up a lease contract in their favor at a fair market rent."
President of the General Court <orig>المحكمة الكلية</orig>

** According to the Description Certificate <orig>شهادة الأوصاف</orig>:

** According to the Expert's Report <orig>تقرير الخبير</orig>:
The first subject of dispute and its on-site inspection located in Al-Rabiya <orig>الرابية</orig>, Block 4, Street (7), House (9), Plot (136), and Automated Number (11810199).
The inspection was carried out as follows:
The subject of dispute is a private residence house overlooking an internal street, a side alley, and a back alley, bordered by one wall. The exterior facade is stone, and the air conditioning type is central. According to the Real Estate Certificate <orig>الشهادة العقارية</orig>, the document number is (1981/468) and its area is 1000 square meters.

First Floor: Consists of (8) bedrooms, (4) bathrooms, a living room, and a balcony.
Second Floor: Consists of two apartments, each comprising (3) bedrooms and (2) bathrooms.
Roof: Maid's room and laundry area.
Basement: Independent as a children's play storage area, consisting of a living room and a storage room.

<page_metadata>
{
  "page_title": "Auction Announcement and Legal Terms for Property Sale <orig>إعلان عن بيع عقار بالمزاد العلني وشروط المزاد</orig>",

<header>
Kuwait Today / Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig> Issue 1733, Seventy-First Year
Sunday, 8 Shawwal 1446 AH - 6/4/2025 AD
71
</header>

The property subject of the dispute consists of a ground floor and a first floor.
During the inspection, it was found that a second floor and a half of a third floor for the elevator were added, with access from one side of the house. These additions are in the black structure stage.
The ground floor consists of a living room and a bathroom, another hall with washbasins and a bathroom, a master bedroom with a bathroom, a main kitchen, and a maid's room with a bathroom.
The first floor consists of a hall with a balcony, a preparatory kitchen, a master bedroom with a bathroom separated by a door, the right side consists of two rooms and a bathroom, and the left side consists of a master bedroom with a bathroom and a room.
The exterior cladding is Jordanian stone.
Air conditioning on the ground floor for the halls is central, and the rest of the floor has units, and the first floor has units.
The flooring of one hall on the ground floor is marble, and the rest of the property's flooring is ceramic.
Mr. Expert <orig>خبير الدرايه</orig> inspected the property and stated that he can estimate the property's value and determine its basic price in preparation for its sale by public auction and submit a report regarding this.

Secondly: Auction Conditions:
First: The auction starts with a basic price of 370,000 KWD (Three Hundred Seventy Thousand Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig>). Participation in the auction requires payment of at least one-fifth of that price by a certified check from the drawee bank or by a letter of guarantee from one of the banks in favor of the Enforcement Department <orig>إدارة التنفيذ</orig> at the Ministry of Justice <orig>وزارة العدل</orig>.
Second: Whoever's bid is approved by the judge must deposit the full approved price, expenses, and registration fees upon the conclusion of the sale session.
Third: If the bidder whose bid was approved does not deposit the full price, they must deposit at least one-fifth of the price; otherwise, the bidding will be re-opened at their expense in the same session based on the price at which the sale was previously awarded.
Fourth: If the bidder deposits the price in the subsequent session, the auction will be awarded to them, unless someone comes forward in that session willing to purchase with a ten percent increase, accompanied by a deposit of the full auction price. In this case, the bidding will be re-opened in the same session based on this new price.
Fifth: If the first bidder does not deposit the full price in the subsequent session and no one comes forward with a ten percent increase, the bidding will immediately be re-opened at their expense based on the price at which it was awarded to them in the previous session. In this session, no bid not accompanied by a full deposit of its value will be considered. The defaulting bidder shall be liable for any shortfall in the property's price.
Sixth: In all cases, the successful bidder shall bear the transfer and registration fees for ownership, enforcement procedure expenses amounting to 200 KWD, legal and expert fees, and advertising and publication costs for the sale in daily newspapers.
Seventh: This announcement is published in accordance with the law, and those directly involved in the sale procedures are responsible for them, without the Clerk's Office <orig>إدارة الكتاب</orig> at the General Court <orig>المحكمة الكلية</orig> bearing any responsibility.
Eighth: The successful bidder acknowledges that they have inspected the property with an inspection that negates ignorance (i.e., a thorough inspection).
Notice:
1- This sale announcement shall be published in the Official Gazette <orig>الجريدة الرسمية</orig> in accordance with Article 266 of the Code of Civil Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig>.
2- The auction award judgment is appealable within seven days from the date of its pronouncement, in accordance with Article 277 of the Code of Civil Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig>.
3- The last paragraph of Article 276 of the Code of Civil Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig> states that "If the dispossessed owner is residing in the property, they shall remain in it as a tenant by force of law, and the successful bidder shall be obligated to draw up a lease contract in their favor at a fair market rent."

Announcement of Property Sale by Public Auction
The Clerk's Office <orig>إدارة الكتاب</orig> at the General Court <orig>المحكمة الكلية</orig> announces the public auction of the property described below, on Thursday, 1/5/2025, in Hall 52, on the second floor of the Palace of Justice <orig>قصر العدل</orig>, at 9:00 AM, in execution of the court judgment issued in lawsuit No. 2024/486 Sales/3
Filed by: Intisar Haji Ali Siral <orig>انتصار حاجي على سيرال</orig>.
Against:
1- Abdullah Ali Abdullah Al-Qablan <orig>عبدالله على عبدالله القبلان</orig>.
2- Director of the Real Estate Registration and Documentation Department <orig>إدارة التسجيل العقاري والتوثيق</orig> in his capacity.
3- Kuwait Credit Bank <orig>بنك الائتمان الكويتي</orig>.
Property Description: According to the attached description certificate.
Property Document No. 1995/17425 located in Al-Qurain <orig>القرين</orig> C 2 - Plot No. (7) Piece No. (5) of Plan No. 36953, with an area of 400 m2
Notes:
*   Violations exist:
    1- Unlicensed elevator installation.
    2- There are large light materials on the first floor facing the street side of the property, which is contrary to the plan.
*   Inspection:

Kuwait Today / Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig> Issue 1733, Seventy-First Year
72
Sunday, 8 Shawwal 1446 AH - 6/4/2025 AD

Filed by: Meshal Rakhees Nasser Al-Dhafiri <orig>مشعل رخيص ناصر الضفيري</orig>.
Against:
First: The heirs of the deceased, namely/ Rakhees Nasser Hadi Al-Dhafiri <orig>رخيص ناصر هادي الضفيري</orig> and the deceased/ Manara Marzouq Yaqoub Al-Dhafiri <orig>مناره مرزوق يعقوب الضفيري</orig>, who are:
1- Ali Rakhees Nasser Al-Dhafiri <orig>عالي رخيص ناصر الضفيري</orig>.
2- Bader Rakhees Nasser Al-Dhafiri <orig>بدر رخيص ناصر الضفيري</orig>.
3- Bandar Rakhees Nasser Al-Dhafiri <orig>بندر رخيص ناصر الضفيري</orig>.
4- Awda Rakhees Nasser Al-Dhafiri <orig>عوده رخيص ناصر الضفيري</orig>.
5- Tarqiyah Rakhees Nasser Al-Dhafiri <orig>طرقييه رخيص ناصر الضفيري</orig>.
6- Latifa Rakhees Nasser Al-Dhafiri <orig>لطيفه رخيص ناصر الضفيري</orig>.
7- Fatma Rakhees Nasser Al-Dhafiri <orig>فطمه رخيص ناصر الضفيري</orig>.
8- Hazna Rakhees Nasser Al-Dhafiri <orig>حزنه رخيص ناصر الضفيري</orig>.
9- Noura Rakhees Nasser Al-Dhafiri <orig>نوره رخيص ناصر الضفيري</orig>.
Second: The heirs of the deceased/ Badriya Rakhees Nasser Al-Dhafiri <orig>بدريه رخيص ناصر الضفيري</orig>.
Third: Talal Hatem Al-Dhafiri <orig>طلال حاتم الضفيري</orig> in his capacity as natural guardian for his children (Bandar <orig>بندر</orig>, Abdulaziz <orig>عبدالعزيز</orig>, Fatima <orig>فاطمة</orig>).
Fourth: Undersecretary of the Ministry of Justice <orig>وزارة العدل</orig> - Real Estate Registration and Authentication Department <orig>إدارة التسجيل العقاري والتوثيق</orig> in his capacity.
Fifth: The Legal Representative of Kuwait Municipality <orig>بلدية الكويت</orig> in his capacity.
First: Property Description: (According to the attached description certificate)
Property Document No. 783/1995 <orig>783/1995</orig> located in Al-Jahra <orig>الجهراء</orig> – Al-Naseem <orig>النسيم</orig> area – Plot No. (256 – Block (1) of Plan No. (M/37003) <orig>م/37003</orig>) with an area of (400m²).
Note:
Violation report No. 25622 <orig>25622</orig> was issued on 1/8/2023 <orig>2023/8/1</orig> for an unlicensed building on the ground floor + a large roof.
*For Inspection:
On 12/4/2023 <orig>2023/4/12</orig>, we moved to Al-Jahra <orig>الجهراء</orig> – Al-Naseem <orig>النسيم</orig> area – Block 1 – Street 28 – Plot No. 256 <orig>256</orig> House 21, in the presence and guidance of the plaintiff personally, with the defendants or their representatives failing to appear, and in the presence of the expert, Professor/ Saad Al-Dukhani <orig>سعد الدخاني</orig>. The inspection was conducted as follows:
- The disputed property is a plot located at the aforementioned address, consisting of a ground floor and a first floor, situated on a main street and a back street, and externally clad with beige stone.
- The expert was unable to inspect the property from the inside after knocking on the door and the house not being opened. It was found by the expert that the main door was locked with an external lock.
- Mr. Expert Professor/ Saad Al-Dukhani <orig>سعد الدخاني</orig> identified the dispute and noted all observations in preparation for estimating the value of the disputed property.
- The expert found that the area of the property is 400 m².
Second: Auction Terms:
First: The auction shall commence with a base price of K.D. 186,988.500 <orig>186988,500 د.ك</orig> (One Hundred Eighty-Six Thousand Nine Hundred Eighty-Eight Kuwaiti Dinars and Five Hundred Fils). Participation in the auction requires payment of at least one-fifth of that price by a certified check from the drawee bank or by a letter of guarantee from one of the banks in favor of the Enforcement Department <orig>إدارة التنفيذ</orig> at the Ministry of Justice <orig>وزارة العدل</orig>.

Second: The bidder whose offer is approved by the judge must deposit the full approved price, expenses, and registration fees at the time of the sale session.
Third: If the bidder whose offer was approved does not deposit the full price, they must deposit at least one-fifth of the price; otherwise, the bidding shall be re-opened at their expense in the same session based on the price at which the sale was previously awarded.
Fourth: If the bidder deposits the price in the subsequent session, the auction shall be awarded to them, unless someone comes forward in that session willing to purchase with a ten percent increase, accompanied by the deposit of the full auction price. In this case, the bidding shall be re-opened in the same session based on this new price.
Fifth: If the first bidder fails to deposit the full price in the subsequent session and no one comes forward to bid with a ten percent increase, the bidding shall immediately be re-opened at their expense based on the price at which it was awarded to them in the previous session. In this session, no offer not accompanied by a full deposit of its value shall be considered, and the defaulting bidder shall be liable for any shortfall in the property's price.
Sixth: In all cases, the successful bidder shall bear the transfer and registration fees for ownership, enforcement procedure expenses amounting to K.D. 200 <orig>200 د.ك</orig>, legal and expert fees, and advertising and publication costs for the sale in daily newspapers.
Seventh: This announcement is published in application of the law, and those directly involved in the sale procedures are responsible for them, without the Clerk's Office <orig>إدارة الكتاب</orig> of the General Court <orig>المحكمة الكلية</orig> bearing any responsibility.
Eighth: The successful bidder acknowledges that they have inspected the property with an inspection that negates ignorance.
Notice:
1- This sale announcement shall be published in the Official Gazette <orig>الجريدة الرسمية</orig> in accordance with Article 266 <orig>266</orig> of the Code of Civil Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig>.
2- The auction award judgment is subject to appeal within seven days from the date of its pronouncement, in accordance with Article 277 <orig>277</orig> of the Code of Civil Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig>.
3- The last paragraph of Article 276 <orig>276</orig> of the Code of Civil Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig> states that "If the dispossessed owner is residing in the property, they shall remain in it as a tenant by operation of law, and the successful bidder shall be obliged to draw up a lease contract in their favor at a fair market rent."
President of the General Court <orig>المحكمة الكلية</orig>

** According to the expert's report <orig>تقرير الخبير</orig>:
On 6/6/2022, the expert team <orig>الخبرة</orig> moved to Sabah Al-Salem <orig>صباح السالم</orig> area, Block 11, Plot 20. In the presence of Mr. Sa'ad Al-Daihani <orig>سعد الديحاني</orig>, the knowledge expert <orig>خبير الدراية</orig>, and with the guidance and enablement of the third and fourth defendants, as the plaintiff failed to attend despite being aware of the session's date, as did the rest of the defendants. The disputed property <orig>عين النزاع</orig> is located on a single internal street, surrounded by neighbors on both sides, and overlooks Main Street No. 207 from the back, named after Mohammed bin Hamada Al-Ajmi <orig>محمد بن حمادة العجمي</orig>.
The disputed property <orig>عين النزاع</orig> is an old government house, consisting of a ground floor, first floor, and a roof, covered with pink Sigma <orig>السيجما</orig> coating. It has two entrances, front and back, and the rear setback is utilized as a garden and parking.
The third defendant enabled the expert team <orig>الخبرة</orig> to enter and inspect, where the following was observed:
- The ground floor consists of a small courtyard overlooking a diwaniya <orig>ديوانية</orig> with a bathroom and washbasins, a driver's room with its entrance from Street No. 1, a kitchen + two bathrooms + two living rooms + a storage room under the stairs.
- The first floor consists of two apartments: the first consists of a master bedroom + small living room + bedroom + bathroom - and the second apartment consists of 3 bedrooms + two bathrooms + kitchen.
- The roof contains a master bedroom.
- The property's finishes are as follows: ceramic floors, regular painted walls, spot lighting and suspended fixtures, and unit air conditioning.
The expert team <orig>الخبرة</orig> and the knowledge expert <orig>خبير الدراية</orig> inspected the property from outside and inside. The knowledge expert also reviewed property document No. 8983, which states that the area of the disputed plot <orig>عين النزاع</orig> is 125,300 m², and also reviewed the sketch plan of the property by the plaintiff's agent in preparation for the necessary valuation of the property according to market price.

<header>
Kuwait Today / Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig> Issue 1733 and Seventy-First Year
Sunday, 8 Shawwal 1446 AH - 2025/4/6 AD
</header>

*Inspection:*
On 2023/3/8, we moved to and inspected the property subject of the lawsuit on site, located in Qurtuba <orig>قرطبة</orig> Area, Plot (2), Street (3), Avenue (4), House (38), bearing automated number (90482719), in the presence and guidance of the plaintiff's agent and the first defendant, and in the presence of Mr. Expert of Knowledge / Osama Al-Ruwaieh <orig>أسامة الرويح</orig> at the time of inspection, as follows:
- The disputed property is a residential plot consisting of a basement, ground floor, first floor, and roof, covered with Jordanian stone, and located on two streets (corner).
- The disputed property conforms to document number 2022/683 and has an area of 587.5 square meters.
- The first defendant provided information on the property's components as follows:
1- The basement consists of a hall + 2 bedrooms + bathroom + office room.
2- The ground floor consists of a hall and reception area + bathroom + refrigerator storage + main kitchen + driver's room with bathroom in the yard and a diwaniya <orig>ديوانية</orig> with bathroom.
3- The first mezzanine consists of 3 bedrooms + 2 bathrooms.
4- The first floor consists of a hall + bedroom + bathroom + kitchen.
5- The second mezzanine consists of 4 bedrooms + bathroom.
6- The roof consists of two bedrooms for workers + bathroom + storage.
7- Central air conditioning.
Secondly: Auction Terms:
First: The auction shall commence with a base price of K.D. 720,000 (Seven Hundred and Twenty Thousand Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig>). Participation in the auction requires payment of at least one-fifth of that price by a certified check from the drawee bank or by a letter of guarantee from one of the banks in favor of the Enforcement Department <orig>إدارة التنفيذ</orig> at the Ministry of Justice <orig>وزارة العدل</orig>.
Second: Whoever's bid is approved by the judge must deposit the full approved price, expenses, and registration fees at the time of the sale session.
Third: If the bidder whose bid was approved does not deposit the full price, they must deposit at least one-fifth of the price; otherwise, the bidding will be re-opened at their expense in the same session based on the price at which the sale was previously awarded.
Fourth: If the bidder deposits the price in the subsequent session, the auction will be awarded to them, unless someone comes forward in that session willing to purchase with a ten percent increase, accompanied by the deposit of the full auction price. In this case, the bidding will be re-opened in the same session based on this new price.
Fifth: If the first bidder fails to deposit the full price in the subsequent session and no one comes forward to bid with a ten percent increase, the bidding will immediately be re-opened at their expense based on the price at which it was awarded to them in the previous session. In this session, no bid not accompanied by a full deposit of its value will be considered. The defaulting bidder is obligated to pay from the property.
Sixth: In all cases, the successful bidder shall bear the transfer and property registration fees, enforcement procedure expenses amounting to K.D. 200, legal and expert fees, and advertising and publication costs for the sale in daily newspapers.
Seventh: This announcement shall be published according to the law, and those directly involved in the sale procedures shall be responsible for them, without the Clerk's Office <orig>إدارة الكتاب</orig> at the General Court <orig>المحكمة الكلية</orig> bearing any responsibility.
Eighth: The successful bidder acknowledges that they have inspected the property in a manner that negates any ignorance.
Notice: 1- This sale announcement shall be published in the Official Gazette <orig>الجريدة الرسمية</orig> according to Article 266 of the Code of Civil Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig>.
2- The auction award judgment is appealable within seven days from the date of its pronouncement, according to Article 277 of the Code of Civil Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig>.
3- The last paragraph of Article 276 of the Code of Civil Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig> states that "If the expropriated owner is residing in the property, they shall remain in it as a tenant by force of law, and the successful bidder is obligated to draw up a lease agreement in their favor at a fair market rent."
President of the General Court <orig>المحكمة الكلية</orig>

Secondly: Auction Terms:
First: The auction shall commence with a base price of 324,000 K.D. (Three Hundred Twenty-Four Thousand Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig>). Participation in the auction requires payment of at least one-fifth of the price by a certified check from the drawee bank or by a letter of guarantee from one of the banks in favor of the Enforcement Department <orig>إدارة التنفيذ</orig> at the Ministry of Justice <orig>وزارة العدل</orig>.
Second: Whoever's bid is approved by the judge must deposit the full approved price, expenses, and registration fees at the time of the sale session.
Third: If the bidder whose bid was approved does not deposit the full price, they must deposit at least one-fifth of the price; otherwise, the bidding will be re-opened at their expense in the same session based on the price at which the sale was previously awarded.
Fourth: If the bidder deposits the price in the subsequent session, the auction will be awarded to them, unless someone comes forward in that session willing to purchase with a ten percent increase, accompanied by the deposit of the full price. In this case, the bidding will be re-opened in the same session based on this new price.
Fifth: If the first bidder fails to deposit the full price in the subsequent session and no one comes forward to bid with the ten percent increase, the bidding will immediately be re-opened at their expense based on the price at which it was awarded to them in the previous session. In this session, no bid not accompanied by the deposit of its full value will be considered. The defaulting bidder shall be liable for any shortfall in the property's price.
Sixth: In all cases, the successful bidder shall bear the transfer and registration fees for ownership, enforcement procedure expenses amounting to 200 K.D., legal and expert fees, and advertising and publication costs for the sale in daily newspapers.
Seventh: This announcement shall be published in accordance with the law, and those directly involved in the sale procedures shall be responsible for them, without the Clerk's Office <orig>إدارة الكتاب</orig> at the General Court <orig>المحكمة الكلية</orig> bearing any responsibility.
Eighth: The successful bidder acknowledges that they have inspected the property in a manner that negates any ignorance.

Notice:
1- This sale announcement shall be published in the Official Gazette <orig>الجريدة الرسمية</orig> in accordance with Article 266 of the Code of Civil Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig>.
2- The auction award judgment is appealable within seven days from the date of its pronouncement, in accordance with Article 277 of the Code of Civil Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig>.
3- The last paragraph of Article 276 of the Code of Civil Procedure <orig>قانون المرافعات</orig> states that "If the dispossessed owner is residing in the property, they shall remain in it as a tenant by operation of law, and the successful bidder shall be obligated to draw up a lease contract in their favor at a fair market rent."
President of the General Court <orig>رئيس المحكمة الكلية</orig>

Announcement of Public Auction for Property Sale
The Clerk's Office <orig>إدارة الكتاب</orig> at the General Court <orig>المحكمة الكلية</orig> announces the public auction of the property described below, on Thursday, 2025/5/1 – Hall 52 – on the second floor of the Palace of Justice <orig>قصر العدل</orig> at 9:00 AM – in execution of the court judgment issued in lawsuit No. 2023/741 Sales/3.
Filed by:
- 1- Shurooq Abdullah Suhaim Al-Hajri <orig>شروق عبدالله سحيم الهاجري</orig>.
- 2- Mai Abdullah Suhaim Al-Hajri <orig>مي عبدالله سحيم الهاجري</orig>.
Against:
- 1- Sheikha Fahad Saqr <orig>شيخة فهد صقر</orig>.
- 2- Faisal Abdullah Suhaim Al-Hajri <orig>فيصل عبدالله سحيم الهاجري</orig>.
- 3- Khalid Abdullah Suhaim Al-Hajri <orig>خالد عبدالله سحيم الهاجري</orig>.
- 4- Munira Abdullah Suhaim Al-Hajri <orig>منيرة عبدالله سحيم الهاجري</orig>.
- 5- Abeer Abdullah Suhaim Al-Hajri <orig>عبير عبدالله سحيم الهاجري</orig>.
- 6- Masha'el Abdullah Suhaim Al-Hajri <orig>مشاعل عبدالله سحيم الهاجري</orig>.
- 7- Nouf Abdullah Suhaim Al-Hajri <orig>نوف عبدالله سحيم الهاجري</orig>.
- 8- Kuwait Credit Bank <orig>بنك الائتمان الكويتي</orig>

First: Property Description according to the attached Certificate of Description.
Property Document No. 1995/9308 located in Jaber Al-Ali <orig>جابر العلي</orig> – Plot 74 – Block 1 – from Plan No. M/36966 – with an area of 392 m².

*Note :
There is a major violation on the rooftop.

*Inspection :
The expert team moved on 2023/9/18 to the disputed property located in Jaber Al-Ali <orig>جابر العلي</orig> Suburb, Block 1, Street 3, House 7, Plot 74, with an area of 392 square meters, in the presence and guidance of the plaintiffs' agent, the second defendant Faisal Al-Hajri <orig>فيصل الهاجري</orig>, and Mr. Osama Al-Ruwaieh <orig>أسامة الرويح</orig>, the knowledge expert, as shown in (Attachment 1 – Inspection Report No. (8)).

Inspection details as follows:
The auctioned property is a house located on a street, with an orange-yellow limestone facade, and has two entrances from the street, one for the diwaniya <orig>ديوانية</orig> and the other for the house courtyard. The property is relatively old.
The second defendant, Faisal <orig>فيصل</orig>, allowed the expert team to enter and inspect the property, and the inspection was as follows:
- The ground floor consists of a living room, a bedroom, a sitting room, a staircase, a main kitchen, a dining room, and a bathroom, and from the outside, a diwaniya <orig>ديوانية</orig> with washbasins and a bathroom.
- The first floor consists of a suite with 2 rooms and 2 bathrooms, and an apartment with 3 rooms, 2 bathrooms, and a hall.
- The second floor, according to the defendant's statement, is identical to the first floor. The expert team was unable to inspect it due to the presence of the family, but it was found from the plans submitted to the expert team that it is identical to the first floor.
- Rooftop: It has a small structure consisting of a room and a bathroom, used for household transactions.

Announcement of Public Auction for Property Sale
The Clerk's Office <orig>إدارة الكتاب</orig> at the General Court <orig>المحكمة الكلية</orig> announces the public auction of the property described below, on Thursday, 2025/5/1 – Hall 52 – on the second floor of the Palace of Justice <orig>قصر العدل</orig> at 9:00 AM – in execution of the court judgment issued in lawsuit No. 2022/775 Sales/3.

for the provision of cleaning workers for Amiri vehicles for the year 2025
The Amiri Diwan <orig>الديوان الأميري</orig> announces the offering of General Practice No. (764/D.M) for the provision of cleaning workers for Amiri vehicles for the year 2025. Those wishing to participate from specialized companies or establishments in this field should apply to obtain the booklet of terms and conditions and practice documents during official working hours from (Amiri Diwan <orig>الديوان الأميري</orig> – Bayan Palace <orig>قصر بيان</orig> – Administrative Building – First Floor – Zone (7) - Tenders and Follow-up Department) during official working hours, starting from the date of publication of the announcement in the Official Gazette (Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig>), for a non-refundable fee of (75 K.D. <orig>د.ك</orig>) only seventy-five Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>ديناراً كويتياً</orig> (K-Net payment only) for the booklet. *   Bids must be submitted in a sealed envelope to the Tenders and Follow-up Department - Bayan Palace <orig>قصر بيان</orig> – Administrative Building – First Floor – Zone 7.
*   Submission of a preliminary guarantee of not less than (2%) in favor of the Amiri Diwan <orig>الديوان الأميري</orig> in the form of a letter of guarantee or a certified check from one of the Kuwaiti banks, valid throughout the bid validity period, which is (90) days.
*   Submission of a valid certificate of compliance with national labor percentage and a valid tax compliance certificate.
*   An authorization letter and a copy of the civil ID for the company representative to purchase the practice document.
*   This practice is indivisible, and alternative offers are not permitted.
*   The bidder must submit a letter attached with a copy of the registration certificate from the Kuwait Chamber of Commerce and Industry <orig>غرفة تجارة وصناعة الكويت</orig>.
*   The preliminary meeting date is Thursday, 10/04/2025, at 11:00 AM.
The bid must remain valid for (90) days from the closing date, while the Amiri Diwan <orig>الديوان الأميري</orig> reserves its right to extend or renew this period for the period(s) it deems appropriate to complete the award procedures.

Auction Announcement No. (2460)
The Ministry of Finance <orig>وزارة المالية</orig> announces the sale of a Lexus LS460L 2010 model vehicle, out of service, by sealed envelope auction, according to the following details:
1- Location for receiving the terms and conditions booklet and auction participation offer: Ministries Complex – Ministry of Finance <orig>وزارة المالية</orig> – Block 11 – Claims and Collections Department – Ground Floor, from 06/04/2025 to 10/04/2025. Documents will be handed over for a non-refundable fee of (30) K.D. <orig>د.ك</orig> payable at the Ministry of Finance <orig>وزارة المالية</orig> treasury.
The bidder will sign, at the time of receiving the terms and conditions booklet, a declaration and undertaking to adhere to the specified deadline for submitting the offer to the Central Sales Committee at the Ministry of Finance <orig>وزارة المالية</orig>.
2- Inspection Date: (5) working days from 06/04/2025 – 10/04/2025. Inspection Time: from 9:00 AM to 12:00 PM.
3- Location for receiving those interested in auction inspection: Ministry of Finance <orig>وزارة المالية</orig> – State Employees Housing Department – Transportation Control in Shuwaikh <orig>الشويخ</orig> area (opposite Al-Bisher Garage <orig>كراج البشر</orig>).
4- Date of Offer Submission and Envelope Opening:
*   Offer submission on Monday, 21/04/2025, at the Ministry of Finance <orig>وزارة المالية</orig> – Ministries Complex – Block 12 – Third Floor – General Storage Affairs Department – Central Sales Department, according to the time specified for the bidder by the Ministry of Finance <orig>وزارة المالية</orig> (No offer will be accepted after the specified time for the bidder has passed).
*   Envelope opening and auction holding on Tuesday, 22/04/2025, at the Ministry of Finance <orig>وزارة المالية</orig> – Ministries Complex – Block 12 – Third Floor – General Storage Affairs Department.
*   Announcement of the successful bidder on the Ministry of Finance <orig>وزارة المالية</orig> website on Tuesday, 22/04/2025.
*   Delivery of checks to bidders who were not awarded the auction on Wednesday, 23/04/2025.
*   The certified check / bank guarantee must be submitted in the name of the Ministry of Finance <orig>وزارة المالية</orig>.
Special Auction Conditions:
1. The bidder must be Kuwaiti – an individual or a company – registered in the Commercial Register and with the Kuwait Chamber of Commerce and Industry <orig>غرفة تجارة وصناعة الكويت</orig>. It may be a foreigner, provided that they have a Kuwaiti partner or commercial agent with a notarized contract. (Must attach: copy of the Commercial and Industrial Register certificate, copy of the company license, copy of the civil ID, authorization letter approved by the Chamber of Commerce and Industry, and they must be valid).
2. Kuwaiti individuals are allowed to participate in the auction (A copy of the civil ID must be attached).
3. The Ministry of Finance <orig>وزارة المالية</orig> is not responsible for transferring vehicle ownership to the successful bidder's name at the Ministry of Interior <orig>وزارة الداخلية</orig>.
To receive the auction terms and conditions booklet: please contact Ms. Fatima Al-Namusi <orig>فاطمة النموسي</orig> and Ms. Sara Al-Kandari <orig>سارة الكندري</orig>
Tel: 99783639 – 22481206
Inspection site official: please contact Mr. Tariq Al-Muqassab <orig>طارق المقصب</orig>, Tel: 99096885
and Mr. Tariq Al-Hussaili <orig>طارق الحصيلي</orig>, Tel: 94407644
Central Sales Committee at the Ministry of Finance <orig>وزارة المالية</orig> / Tel: (22481971)
Website address: www.mof.gov.kw
Undersecretary of the Ministry of Finance <orig>وزارة المالية</orig>

Announcement
Regarding Practice No. MWTAFA – (2) / 2026/2025
Maintenance of Security Surveillance Camera Systems and their Accessories for the Sites of
the National Council for Culture, Arts and Letters <orig>المجلس الوطني للثقافة والفنون والآداب</orig>

Specialized companies wishing to participate in this practice must obtain the practice documents for a non-refundable fee of (75 K.D.) only seventy-five Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig> from the Financial Affairs Department <orig>إدارة الشئون المالية</orig> – Contracts Section <orig>قسم العقود</orig> – Second Floor – National Council for Culture, Arts and Letters <orig>المجلس الوطني للثقافة والفنون والآداب</orig> Building – Martyrs Street <orig>شارع الشهداء</orig> – Sharq <orig>الشرق</orig>.

All documents must be submitted on a (CD) in 3 copies, with the exception of (the bid form, preliminary insurance/bid bond, a copy of the purchase receipt, and the bidder's form).
The bidding is indivisible, and no alternative offers will be accepted.
