# Capital Markets Authority <orig>هيئة أسواق المال</orig>

### Announcement

The Capital Markets Authority <orig>هيئة أسواق المال</orig> announces the end of the period for delivering clients' funds and assets to them or to those related to their possession, management, or safekeeping for Al-Madina for Finance and Investment Company <orig>شركة المدينة للتمويل والاستثمار</orig>.
The end of this period does not absolve Al-Madina for Finance and Investment Company <orig>شركة المدينة للتمويل والاستثمار</orig>, or Mr. / Saleh Nasser Saleh Al-Saleh <orig>صالح ناصر صالح الصالح</orig>, the Vice Chairman of the Company's Board of Directors, or its Board of Directors, from any current or future legal responsibility related to contracts concluded with its clients, or related to the process of delivering their funds and assets to them or to those related to their possession, management, or safekeeping, towards the clients of Al-Madina for Finance and Investment Company <orig>شركة المدينة للتمويل والاستثمار</orig> or third parties.
The end of this period shall not be considered in any way an endorsement by the Capital Markets Authority <orig>هيئة أسواق المال</orig>, or a basis for the validity of the process of delivering clients' funds and assets to them or to those related to their possession, management, or safekeeping, or for the clearance of Al-Madina for Finance and Investment Company's <orig>شركة المدينة للتمويل والاستثمار</orig> dealings with its clients or with third parties.

  "page_summary": "This page of the Kuwait Today official gazette contains several announcements from the Central Agency for Public Tenders, including results of a technical support tender, postponement of deadlines for mosque renovation and refrigeration supply tenders, and details for a new tender for air navigation services at Kuwait International Airport."

<header>
Kuwait Today / Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig> Issue 1733, Seventy-First Year
Sunday, 8 Shawwal 1446 AH - 06/04/2025 AD
82
</header>
The initial guarantee amounts to (K.D. 5,170) and must be valid throughout the tender validity period and issued in the name of the Central Agency for Information Technology <orig>الجهاز المركزي لتكنولوجيا المعلومات</orig>.
Please bring the following documents to obtain the terms and conditions booklet:
1. Valid registration certificate with the Central Agency for Public Tenders <orig>الجهاز المركزي للمناقصات العامة</orig>.
2. Valid registration certificate with the Central Agency for Information Technology <orig>الجهاز المركزي لتكنولوجيا المعلومات</orig>.
3. Valid certificate from the Public Authority for Civil Information <orig>الهيئة العامة للمعلومات المدنية</orig> (Civil Entity Number).
4. Valid national labor percentage fulfillment certificate.
5. Authorization letter and a copy of the civil ID for the company's representative to purchase the booklet.

All documents must be submitted on a non-copyable CD, except for the tender format and initial insurance, which must be submitted as hard copies.
A valid national labor percentage fulfillment certificate issued by the Public Authority for Manpower <orig>الهيئة العامة للقوى العاملة</orig> must be submitted with the tender.
In accordance with Article 48 of Public Tenders Law No. 49 of 2016, which stipulates:
"Tender envelopes shall be opened at the time and place specified in the tender documents in a public session attended by the tenderers or their representatives."
The practice documents will be published on the Agency's website for review before proceeding to purchase the documents. In case of purchasing the documents and paying the prescribed fees, requests for fee refunds will not be accepted except in the event of the practice's cancellation in accordance with the provisions of Article (55) of the Public Tenders Law.
This announcement serves as an invitation for interested practitioners to attend, as interested companies have the right to attend the envelope opening session.
Interested companies wishing to attend must coordinate with the Tender Opening Department <orig>قسم فض العطاءات</orig> before the scheduled date of the tender opening session and bring the following documents: -
1. Copy of the civil ID.
2. Copy of the signature authorization for the Central Agency for Public Tenders <orig>الجهاز المركزي للمناقصات العامة</orig>.
3. If someone other than the authorized signatory attends, a written letter of authorization from the authorized signatory at the Central Agency for Public Tenders <orig>الجهاز المركزي للمناقصات العامة</orig> must be presented, delegating whomever they deem fit to attend the session.
This announcement is considered an integral part of the practice documents.
For more information, please visit our website WWW.CAPT.GOV.KW
Secretary General of the Central Agency for Public Tenders <orig>الجهاز المركزي للمناقصات العامة</orig>

Based on Article (19) of Municipality <orig>البلدية</orig> Resolution No. (2009/161) regarding the classification, licensing, and registration of construction and demolition contractors in Kuwait Municipality <orig>بلدية الكويت</orig>, which stipulates that a contractor may submit a request to the Municipality <orig>البلدية</orig> to cancel their registration before its expiry or to cancel the classification, and the committee stipulated in Article (1) of this regulation may issue its decision to that effect after fulfilling the following two conditions:
1- The contractor has completed all contracted works.
2- The lapse of fifteen (15) days from the date of publishing this request in the Official Gazette <orig>الجريدة الرسمية</orig>.
The cancellation of the license or registration entails the return of the bank guarantee submitted by the contractor, taking into account the last paragraph of Article (10) of this resolution.
Accordingly, the Municipality <orig>البلدية</orig> appeals to anyone who has any claims against the aforementioned contractor regarding construction contracting agreements concluded between them that have not yet been completed, or judicial attachments in their favor due to violating contracting works or dues arising from the contracting agreement, to review the Contractors Department at the Engineering Systems Department within a maximum period of fifteen days from this date. The Municipality <orig>البلدية</orig> will not consider any claims submitted after the prescribed period.
Director General of the Municipality <orig>مدير عام البلدية</orig>

- This announcement is considered as an invitation for the willing tenderers, who are qualified by CAPT, to attend the opening of the bids envelopes, as the desired companies are entitled to attend.
- Companies wishing to attend should coordinate with the Bid Opening Department before the day mentioned for the bid opening session and should bring the following documents:
.1 Copy of Civil ID
.2 A copy of the authorized signatory of CAPT.
.3 In case that someone is present other than the person authorized to sign, a written letter must be brought from the authorized person, whom signature is approved by CAPT, authorizing whomever he sees fit to attend the session.
- This declaration is considered an integral part of the tender documentation.

As for a person who has a share in separate companies, each independent with its legal personality, financial resources, engineers, employees, and administrative qualifications, they may, upon classification, register themselves and each of their independent companies. Any bid from a tenderer that violates this article shall be deemed null and void by judgment.
* For any inquiries or requests related to the tender documents, these must be sent in writing via email no later than 10:00 AM on the day following the preliminary meeting. Requests submitted after this deadline will not be considered for any reason.
* The value of the tender documents is non-refundable.
* The preliminary bond must be valid throughout the bid validity period (90 days from the closing date) and submitted in favor of the Higher Purchasing Committee for Tenders of Kuwait Petroleum Corporation <orig>مؤسسة البترول الكويتية</orig> and its subsidiaries.
* Bids must be addressed with the tender name and number and placed in the special bid box located at the headquarters of Kuwait Petroleum Corporation <orig>مؤسسة البترول الكويتية</orig> - Oil Sector Complex - Shuwaikh <orig>الشويخ</orig> - Arabian Gulf Street <orig>شارع الخليج العربي</orig> - (Waiting Room) - next to Gate No. (1) before the aforementioned closing time. * The tenderer must be registered on the website of Kuwait Petroleum Corporation <orig>مؤسسة البترول الكويتية</orig> and its subsidiaries (ktendering.com.kw) and must submit a certificate proving this with the bid.
* It is a condition for those wishing to participate in the tender to send a participation request via email (purch_contracts@kpc.com.kw) with only one PDF file attached, containing the following documents in the specified order:
1. A letter addressed to Kuwait Petroleum Corporation <orig>مؤسسة البترول الكويتية</orig> from the authorized signatory expressing the desire to participate, including the company's details as follows:
   Name of the person responsible for coordination between the Corporation and the tenderer.
   Direct phone number (mobile + landline).
   Email address (for the person + for the company).
   Fax number.
   Company address.
2. An official letter from the authorized signatory including the following:
   Names of persons authorized to sign on behalf of the company.
   Their job titles.
   Phone numbers (mobile + landline).
   Email addresses.
3. A copy of a valid certificate of compliance with the national labor percentage for non-governmental entities, issued and approved by the Public Authority for Manpower <orig>الهيئة العامة للقوى العاملة</orig>.
4. A copy of the company's articles of association in addition to the latest amendment contract (if any).
5. A copy of the commercial license from the Ministry of Commerce and Industry <orig>وزارة التجارة والصناعة</orig>.
6. A recent letter (no older than 2022) containing the signature specimen of the person authorized to sign on behalf of the company, attested by the Kuwait Chamber of Commerce and Industry <orig>غرفة تجارة وصناعة الكويت</orig>.
7. A copy of a valid registration certificate with the Kuwait Chamber of Commerce and Industry <orig>غرفة تجارة وصناعة الكويت</orig>.
8. A copy of a valid registration certificate with the Central Agency for Public Tenders <orig>الجهاز المركزي للمناقصات العامة</orig>.
9. A copy of a valid registration certificate with the Central Agency for Information Technology <orig>الجهاز المركزي لتكنولوجيا المعلومات</orig>.

# General Fire Force <orig>قوة الإطفاء العام</orig>
## Announcement
Tender Practice No. (2024/24/25)
The General Fire Force <orig>قوة الإطفاء العام</orig> announces the tender practice No. (2024/24/25) for the transfer of Marine Firefighting Department employees from Salmiya <orig>السالمية</orig> Marine Rescue Center to Failaka <orig>فيلكا</orig> Marine Rescue Center, affiliated with the General Fire Force <orig>قوة الإطفاء العام</orig>, for a period of two years.
Specialists in this field are requested to refer to the Accounting Department (Cashier) at the General Fire Force <orig>قوة الإطفاء العام</orig> in Mubarak Al-Abdullah <orig>مبارك العبد الله</orig> area, Second Floor, to obtain the special specifications for a fee of (75 K.D.) only seventy-five Kuwaiti Dinars <orig>دينار كويتي</orig> – non-refundable – bringing with them the following documents:
1. Copy of the Commercial Register.
2. Copy of the Kuwait Chamber of Commerce and Industry <orig>غرفة تجارة وصناعة الكويت</orig> certificate.
3. Copy of the registration receipt with the Central Agency for Public Tenders <orig>الجهاز المركزي للمناقصات العامة</orig>.
4. Copy of the certificate of compliance with the national labor percentage for non-governmental companies, issued by the Ministry of Social Affairs and Labor <orig>وزارة الشؤون الاجتماعية والعمل</orig> and valid for one year, to be submitted with the bid.
5. Copy of the supplier registration receipt with the General Fire Force <orig>قوة الإطفاء العام</orig>.
6. Security deposit value: 2% of the submitted bid value.
7. Preliminary meeting on Thursday, 2025/4/17.
8. Bids to be submitted to the Tenders and Contracts Preparation Department at the General Fire Force <orig>قوة الإطفاء العام</orig> in Mubarak Al-Abdullah <orig>مبارك العبد الله</orig> area (West Mishref <orig>غرب مشرف</orig>), First Floor.

Steam Tracing for Sulphur Tanks - TK-23-101/102/103/104 in MAB Refinery
In accordance with the general and special terms and conditions stipulated in the tender documents. These documents can be obtained by visiting the unified electronic commercial platform (K-Tendering portal) on the website of Kuwait Petroleum Corporation <orig>مؤسسة البترول الكويتية</orig> and its subsidiaries:
((https://ktendering.com.kw))

The final deadline for submitting bids is Thursday, 5/6/2025, at 1:00 PM local time of the State of Kuwait <orig>دولة الكويت</orig> (13:00 Noon), noting that bids must be submitted through the electronic commercial platform mentioned above.
*   The bidder must submit the initial security in favor of Kuwait National Petroleum Company <orig>شركة البترول الوطنية الكويتية</orig> in an envelope clearly marked with the tender name, address, and closing date. It should be placed in the designated box located on the first floor, reception hall, at the Kuwait National Petroleum Company <orig>شركة البترول الوطنية الكويتية</orig> Head Office building in Al-Ahmadi <orig>الأحمدي</orig>, no later than 1:00 PM (13:00 Noon) on Thursday, 5/6/2025, with a copy of the initial security attached to the bid.
*   The bidder must deposit the tender document purchase fee into the account of Kuwait National Petroleum Company <orig>شركة البترول الوطنية الكويتية</orig>:
(KW59NBOK00000000000002004811204)
and submit the receipt with the bid. Bids not accompanied by the payment receipt will be rejected. If the bid is submitted electronically, a copy of the payment receipt must be attached electronically with the bid.
*   Please note that this tender is restricted and non-divisible among the companies listed in the attached list.
*   Please note that a preliminary meeting for bidders will be held remotely (online via MS Teams application) at 10:00 AM on Monday, 21/4/2025, to answer bidders' inquiries. The meeting link - and other details for joining the meeting - will be sent to all bidders through the electronic commercial platform (K-Tendering portal), which bidders should regularly monitor for updates regarding the tender.
*   No single person or group of persons combined may register under more than one name during classification, or submit more than one bid in a tender, except for alternative bids where the tender conditions permit their submission.
However, a person who has a share in separate companies, each independent with its legal personality, finances, engineers, employees, and general administrative apparatus, may, during classification, register himself and each of his independent companies. Any bid from a bidder violating this article shall be deemed null and void by operation of law, in accordance with Article No. (29) of Law No. (49) of 2016 regarding Public Tenders <orig>المناقصات العامة</orig>.
Note: -
*   All required documents and certificates must be attached to the bid through the electronic commercial platform as specified in the tender documents.
*   The Supreme Purchasing Committee <orig>لجنة الشراء العليا</orig> wishes to draw the attention of Messrs./Bidders who have inquiries or reservations regarding the technical specifications to submit such requests at most (three weeks) before the closing date (for this tender). These requests will be rejected and will not be considered for any reason after this deadline.

Announcement

The Higher Purchasing Committee <orig>لجنة الشراء العليا</orig>, upon the request of Kuwait National Petroleum Company <orig>شركة البترول الوطنية الكويتية</orig> – one of the subsidiaries of Kuwait Petroleum Corporation <orig>مؤسسة البترول الكويتية</orig> – announces the issuance of Practice No.: RFQ/1055241 – MAA-DC BARE SHAFT PUMP, along with the general and special specifications contained in the practice documents. *   The last date for submitting bids is Thursday, 2025/5/1, at 1:00 PM local time of the State of Kuwait <orig>دولة الكويت</orig> (13:00 Noon), noting that bid submission must be through the electronic commercial platform mentioned above.
*   The bidder must submit the initial security deposit in favor of Kuwait National Petroleum Company <orig>شركة البترول الوطنية الكويتية</orig> in an envelope inscribed with the name and address of the practice and the closing date. It should be placed in the designated box located on the first floor, reception hall, Kuwait National Petroleum Company <orig>شركة البترول الوطنية الكويتية</orig> Main Office building in Ahmadi <orig>الأحمدي</orig>, no later than 1:00 PM (13:00 Noon) on Thursday, 2025/5/1, with a copy of the initial security deposit attached to the bid.
*   The bidder must deposit the document purchase fee into the account of Kuwait National Petroleum Company <orig>شركة البترول الوطنية الكويتية</orig>: (KW59NBOK000000000000002004811204).
*   The receipt must be submitted with the bid. Bids not accompanied by the payment receipt will be excluded. In case of electronic bid submission, a copy of the payment receipt must be attached electronically with the bid.
*   Please note that this practice is general and divisible, where supply shall be from the manufacturer mentioned in the practice documents.
*   No single person or group of persons combined may register under more than one name during classification, or submit more than one bid in a tender. This excludes alternative bids where the tender conditions permit their submission.
*   A person who has a share in separate companies, each independent of the other and each company being independent in its legal personality, finances, engineering, employees, and general administrative apparatus, may, during classification, register himself and each of his independent companies.

> Please note that this tender is general and indivisible, such that the supply must be from the manufacturer mentioned in the tender documents.
> It is not permissible for one person or a group of persons combined to register under more than one name during classification, or to submit more than one bid in a tender, except for alternative bids where the tender conditions allow their submission.
However, a person who has a share in separate companies, where each company is independent with its legal personality, finances, engineers, employees, and general administrative apparatus, may, during classification, register himself and each of his independent companies.
The bid of a tenderer who violates this article shall be deemed null and void by operation of law, in accordance with Article No. (29) of Law No. (49) of 2016 regarding Public Tenders <orig>المناقصات العامة</orig>.
Note:
> All required documents and certificates must be attached to the bid through the electronic commercial platform as specified in the tender documents.
> The Supreme Procurement Committee <orig>لجنة الشراء العليا</orig> wishes to draw the attention of the esteemed bidders/practitioners who have inquiries or reservations regarding the technical specifications to submit such requests at most (two weeks) before the closing date (for this tender). These requests will be rejected and will not be considered for any reason whatsoever after this deadline.
> To obtain a username and password for accessing the commercial platform, please contact the following phone numbers: 23887794 / 23887792.
cwphelp@knpc.com
> Illustrative guidelines on how to submit a bid through the electronic commercial platform are available on our website.
<footer>
Secretary of the Committee <orig>أمين السر</orig>
Note: -
- All required documents and certificates must be attached to the bid through the electronic commercial platform as specified in the tender documents.
</footer>

  1. Determining all required conditions by the Public Institution for Social Security <orig>المؤسسة العامة للتأمينات الاجتماعية</orig> and other entities.
2.  Evaluating job tasks on scientific bases to measure risks / derived risks using specialized equipment.
3.  Identifying sources and causes of risks and the degree of employee exposure to risks / derived risks.
4.  Writing a complete job description containing information about risks / derived risks for each job included in this study.
5.  Conducting a field survey and measurements that require variables to measure risks.
    Example (exposure to physical pollutants, chemical pollutants, biological pollutants)
6.  Obtaining final accreditation from the Public Institution for Social Security <orig>المؤسسة العامة للتأمينات الاجتماعية</orig>.

## Announcement
### Annual Plan for Supply, Contracting, and Services Contracts

Kuwait Oil Company <orig>شركة نفط الكويت</orig> announces that, in accordance with Article No. (33) and Article No. (88) of Public Tenders Law No. 49/2016 <orig>قانون المناقصات العامة رقم 2016/49</orig> regarding the subject of the above-mentioned announcement, plans are published weekly on the official website of Kuwait Oil Company <orig>شركة نفط الكويت</orig>. Therefore, all those wishing to view them should visit the website continuously to obtain the latest updates through the following steps:
1- Company Website WWW.KOCW.COM
2- Click on E-business
3- Select one of the options: Tenders (RFPs) and Purchases (RFQs).
4- Click on Upcoming

- We would also like to draw the attention of the esteemed bidders/companies that, based on the text of Article (29) of Public Tenders Law 2016 <orig>قانون المناقصات العامة 2016</orig> regarding public tenders, "It is not permissible for one person or a group of persons combined to register under more than one name during classification or to submit more than one bid in a tender, except for alternative bids where the tender conditions allow their submission. However, a person who has a share in separate companies, each independent in its legal personality, finances, engineering, employees, and general administrative apparatus, may register himself and each of his independent companies during classification. The bid of a bidder who violates this article shall be considered null and void by operation of law."

## Announcement
### Pre-offering of Limited Tenders to a List of Companies

The Higher Purchase Committee for Tenders of Kuwait Petroleum Corporation <orig>مؤسسة البترول الكويتية</orig> and its Subsidiaries announces, upon the request of Kuwait Oil Company <orig>شركة نفط الكويت</orig>, the offering of Tender No.: RFP- 2106873
**SEISMIC DATA PROCESSING SERVICES**

In this regard, we draw attention to the fact that, based on the text of Article (16) of Tenders Law No. (49) of 2016 <orig>قانون المناقصات رقم (49) لسنة 2016</orig> regarding public tenders, the above-mentioned tender/practice will be offered to the following list of companies, numbering (30), at least (30) days after the date of publication of this announcement in the Official Gazette (Kuwait Today / Al-Kuwait Al-Youm <orig>الكويت اليوم</orig>) and on the company's website. Any interested party whose name is not included in the list of invited companies for the tender has the right to appeal their exclusion or submit a request to participate in the tender, accompanied by supporting documents and addressed to Mr. / Chairman of the Higher Purchase Committee for Tenders of Kuwait Petroleum Corporation <orig>مؤسسة البترول الكويتية</orig> and its Subsidiaries, within (30) days from the date of this announcement.

|:--------|:---|:---|
| 1       | ANTON OILFIELD SERVICES DMCC | CAT-35A & 35B |
| 2       | OPTIMUM ENGINEERING STANDARDS CO. LTD. | Approved in KOC CAT-35A & 35B |
</table>

Hence, this notice is issued.
For any additional information, please visit the official website of Kuwait Oil Company <orig>شركة نفط الكويت</orig> through the commercial electronic page (K-Tendering Portal) on the website of Kuwait Petroleum Corporation <orig>مؤسسة البترول الكويتية</orig> and its Subsidiaries:
https://www.ktendering.com.kw
